sūryasya vaṃśaḥ kathito mayā mune samudgatā yatra nareśvarāḥ purā 
mayocyamānāñ chaśinaḥ samāhitaḥ śṛṇuṣva vaṃśe atha nṛpān anuttamān ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sūryavaṃśakathanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।

somavaṃśaṃ śṛṇuṣvātha bharadvāja mahāmune 
purāṇe vistareṇoktaṃ saṃkṣepāt kathaye adhunā ।। 

ādau tāvad brahmā । brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putro marīcir marīcer dākṣāyaṇyāṃ dākṣāyiṇyāṃ kaśyapaḥ ।। 

kaśyapād aditer ādityaḥ । ādityāt suvarṇalāyāṃ manuḥ ।। 

ḥmanor surūpāyāṃ somaḥ ।
ḥsomād rohiṇyāṃ budhaḥ ।
ḥbudhād ilāyāṃ purūravāḥ ।। 

purūravasa āyuḥ । āyo rūpavatyāṃ nahuṣaḥ ।। 

nahuṣāt pitṛvatyāṃ yayātiḥ । yayāteḥ śarmiṣṭhāyāṃ pūruḥ ।। 

ḥpūror vaṃśadāyāṃ saṃpātiḥ ।
ḥsaṃpāter bhānudattāyāṃ sārvabhaumaḥ ।
ḥsārvabhaumasya vaidehyāṃ bhojaḥ ।। 

bhojasya liṅgāyāṃ duṣyantaḥ । duṣyantasya śakuntalāyāṃ bharataḥ ।। 

bharatasya nandāyām ajamīḍhaḥ । ajamīḍhasya sudevyāṃ pṛśniḥ । pṛśner ugrasenāyāṃ prasaraḥ । 
ḥprasarasya bahurūpāyāṃ śaṃtanuḥ ।
ḥśaṃtanor yojanagandhāyāṃ vicitravīryaḥ ।
ḥvicitravīryasyāmbikāyāṃ pāṇḍuḥ ।। 
pāṇḍoḥ kuntidevyām arjunaḥ । arjunāt subhadrāyām abhimanyuḥ ।। 

ḥabhimanyor uttarāyāṃ parīkṣitaḥ ।
ḥparīkṣitasya mātṛvatyāṃ janamejayaḥ ।
ḥjanamejayasya puṇyavatyāṃ śatānīkaḥ ।। 

ḥśatānīkasya puṣpavatyāṃ sahasrānīkaḥ ।
ḥsahasrānīkasya mṛgavatyām udayanaḥ ।
ḥtasya vāsavadattāyāṃ naravāhanaḥ ।। 

naravāhanasyāśvamedhāyāṃ kṣemakaḥ । kṣemakāntāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ somavaṃśo nivartate ।। 

ya idaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ rājavaṃśam anuttamam 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 

yaś cedaṃ paṭhate nityaṃ śrāddhe vā śrāvayet pitṝn 
vaṃśānukīrtanaṃ puṇyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam ।। 

rājñāṃ hi somasya mayā taveritā vaṃśānukīrtir dvija pāpanāśanī 
śṛṇuṣva viprendra mayocyamānaṃ manvantaraṃ cāpi caturdaśākhyam ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe somavaṃśānukīrtanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

prathamaṃ tāvat svāyaṃbhuvaṃ manvantaraṃ tatsvarūpaṃ kathitam । sargādau svārociṣo nāma dvitīyo manuḥ ।। 

tasmin svārociṣe manvantare vipaścin nāma devendraḥ । pārāvatāḥ satuṣitā devāḥ ।। 

ūrjastambaḥ suprāṇo danto nirṛṣabho varīyān īśvaraḥ somaḥ saptarṣayaś caivaṃ kiṃpuruṣādyāḥ svārociṣasya manoḥ putrā rājāno bhavanti ।। 

ḥtṛtīya uttamo nāma manuḥ ।
ḥsudhāmānaḥ satyāḥ śivāḥ pratardanā vaṃśavartinaś ca devāḥ ।
ḥpañcaite dvādaśagaṇāḥ ।। 

teṣāṃ suśāntir indraḥ ।। 

vandyāḥ saptarṣayo abhavan । atra paraśucitrādyā manoḥ sutāḥ ।। 

caturthas tāmaso nāma manuḥ । tatra manvantare surāḥ parāḥ satyā sudhiyaś ca saptaviṃśatikā gaṇāḥ ।। 

tatra bhṛśuṇḍī nāma devendraḥ । hiraṇyaromā devaśrīr ūrdhvabāhur devabāhuḥ sudhāmā ha parjanyo munir ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। 

jyotirdhāmā pṛthuḥ kāśyo agnir dhanaka ity ete tāmasasya manoḥ putrā rājānaḥ ।। 

pañcamo nāma raivato manuḥ । 
ḥtasyāntare amitā niratā vaikuṇṭhāḥ sumedhasa ity ete devagaṇāś caturdaśakā gaṇāḥ ।
ḥasurāntako nāma devendraḥ ।
ḥsaptakādyā manoḥ sutā rājāno vai babhūvuḥ ।। 
śāntaḥ śāntabhayo vidvāṃs tapasvī medhāvī sutapāḥ saptarṣayo abhavan ।। 

ḥṣaṣṭhaś cākṣuṣo nāma manuḥ ।
ḥpuruśatadyumnapramukhās tasya sutā rājānaḥ ।
ḥsuśāntā āpyāḥ prasūtā bhavyāḥ prathitāś ca mahānubhāvāḥ lekhādyāḥ pañcaite hy aṣṭakā gaṇās tatra devāḥ ।। 

teṣām indro manojavaḥ । medhāḥ sumedhā virajā haviṣmān uttamo matimān nāmnā sahiṣṇuś caite saptarṣayaḥ ।। 

saptamo vaivasvato manuḥ sāṃprataṃ vartate । tasya putrā ikṣvākuprabhṛtayaḥ kṣatriyā bhūbhujaḥ ।। 

ādityaviśvavasurudrādyā devāḥ puraṃdaro atra devendraḥ ।। 

vaśiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapo atrir jamadagnir gautamaviśvāmitrabharadvājāḥ saptarṣayo bhavanti ।। 

ḥbhaviṣyāṇi manvantarāṇi kathyante ।
ḥtad yathā ādityāt saṃjñāyāṃ jāto yo manuḥ pūrvoktaś chāyāyām utpanno manur dvitīyaḥ sa tu ।
ḥpūrvajasya sāvarṇasya manvantaraṃ sāvarṇikam aṣṭamaṃ śṛṇu ।। 

manuḥ sāvarṇo aṣṭamo bhavitā tatra sutapādyā devagaṇās teṣāṃ balir indro bhavitā ।। 

dīptimān gālavo nāma kṛpadrauṇivyāsarṣyaśṛṅgāś ca saptarṣayo bhavitāraḥ । virājorvarīyanirmokādyāḥ sāvarṇasya manoḥ sutā rājāno bhaviṣyanti ।। 

navamo dakṣasāvarṇir manur bhavitā । dhṛtiḥ kīrtir dīptiḥ ketuḥ pañcahasto nirāmayaḥ pṛthuśravādyā dakṣasāvarṇā rājāno asya manoḥ putrāḥ ।। 

marīcigarbhāḥ sudharmāṇo haviṣmantas tatra devatāḥ । teṣāṃ indro adbhutaḥ ।। 

savanaḥ kṛtimān havyo vasumedhātithir jyotiṣmān ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। 

daśamo brahmasāvarṇir manur bhavitā । 
ḥviruddhādayas tatra devāḥ ।
ḥteṣāṃ śāntir indraḥ ।
ḥhaviṣmān sukṛtiḥ satyas tapomūrtir nābhāgaḥ pratimokaḥ saptaketur ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। 
sukṣetra uttamo bhūriṣeṇādayo brahmasāvarṇiputrā rājāno bhaviṣyanti ।। 

ekādaśe manvantare dharmasāvarṇiko manuḥ ।। 

siṃhasavanādayo devagaṇāḥ । teṣāṃ divaspatir indraḥ ।। 

nirmohas tattvadarśī nikaṃpo nirutsāho dhṛtimān rucya ity ete saptarṣayaḥ । citrasenavicitrādyā dharmasāvarṇiputrā bhūbhṛto bhaviṣyanti ।। 

rudrasāvarṇir bhavitā dvādaśo manuḥ ।। 

kṛtadhāmā tatrendro haritā rohitāḥ sumanasaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sutapāś ca devāḥ ।। 

tapasvī cārutapās tapomūrtis taporatis tapodhṛtir jyotis tapa ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। 

devavān devaśreṣṭhādyās tasya manoḥ sutā bhūpālā bhaviṣyanti ।। 

ḥtrayodaśo rucir nāma manuḥ ।
ḥsragvī bāṇaḥ sudharmā prabhṛtayo devagaṇāḥ ।
ḥteṣām indra ṛṣabho nāma bhavitā ।। 

niścito agnitejā vapuṣmān dhṛṣṭo vāruṇir haviṣmān nahuṣo bhavya iti saptarṣayaḥ । sudharmā devānīkādayas tasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthvīśvarā bhaviṣyanti ।। 

ḥbhaumaś caturdaśo manur bhavitā ।
ḥsurucis tatrendraḥ ।
ḥcakṣuṣmantaḥ pavitrāḥ kaniṣṭhābhā devagaṇāḥ ।। 

agnibāhuśuciśukramādhavaśivābhīmajitaśvāsā ity ete saptarṣayaḥ । urugaṃbhīrabrahmādyās tasya manoḥ sutāḥ rājanaḥ ।। 

evaṃ te caturdaśa manvantarāṇi kathitāni । rājānaś ca yair iyaṃ vasudhā pālyate ।। 

manuḥ saptarṣayo devā bhūpālāś ca manoḥ sutāḥ 
manvantare bhavanty ete śakrāś caivādhikāriṇaḥ ।। 

caturdaśabhir etais tu gatair manvantarair dvija 
sahasrayugaparyantaḥ kālo gacchati vāsaraḥ ।। 

tāvatpramāṇā ca niśā tato bhavati sattama 
brahmarūpadharaḥ śete sarvātmā nṛhariḥ svayam ।। 

trailokyam akhilaṃ grastā bhagavān ādikṛd vibhuḥ 
svamāyām āsthito vipra sarvarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। 

atha prabuddho bhagavān yathā pūrvaṃ tathā punaḥ 
yugavyavasthāṃ kurute sṛṣṭiṃ ca puruṣottamaḥ ।। 

ete tavoktā manavo amarāś ca putrāś ca bhūpā munayaś ca sarve 
vibhūtayas tasya sthitau sthitasya tasyaiva sarvaṃ tvam avehi vipra ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe trayoviṃśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vaṃśānucaritaṃ śubham 
śṛṇvatām api pāpaghnaṃ sūryasomanṛpātmakam ।। 

sūryavaṃśodbhavo yo vai manuputraḥ puroditaḥ 
ikṣvākur nāma bhūpālaś caritaṃ tasya me śṛṇu ।। 

āsīd bhūmau mahābhāga purī divyā suśobhanā 
sarayūtīram āsādya ayodhyā nāma nāmataḥ ।। 

amarāvatyatiśayā triṃśadyojanajālinī 
hastyaśvarathapattyoghair drumaiḥ kalpadrumaprabhaiḥ ।। 

prākārāṭṭapratolībhis toraṇaiḥ kāñcanaprabhaiḥ 
virājamānā sarvatra suvibhaktacatuṣpathā ।। 

anekabhūmiprāsādā bahubhāṇḍasuvikrayā 
padmotpalaśubhais toyair vāpībhir upaśobhitā ।। 

devatāyatanair divyair vedaghoṣaiś ca śobhitā 
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgaiś ca śabdair utkṛṣṭakair yutā ।। 

śālais tālair nālikeraiḥ panasāmalajambukaiḥ 
tathaivāmrakapitthādyair aśokair upaśobhitā ।। 

ārāmair vividhair yuktā sarvatra phalapādapaiḥ 
mallikāmālatījātipāṭalānāgacampakaḥ ।। 

karavīraiḥ karṇikāraiḥ ketakībhir alaṃkṛtā 
kadalīlavalījātimātuluṅgamahāphalaiḥ 
kvacic candanagandhādyair nāraṅgaiś ca suśobhitā ।। 

nityotsavapramuditā gītavādyavicakṣaṇaiḥ 
naranārībhir āḍhyābhī rūpadraviṇaprekṣaṇaiḥ ।। 

nānājanapadākīrṇā patākādhvajaśobhitā 
devatulyaprabhāyuktair nṛpaputraiś ca saṃyutā ।। 

sarūpābhir varastrībhir devastrībhir ivāvṛtā 
vipraiḥ satkavibhir yuktā bṛhaspatisamaprabhaiḥ ।। 

vaṇigjanais tathā pauraiḥ kalpavṛkṣavarair yutā 
aśvair uccaiḥśravastulyair dantibhir diggajair iva ।। 

iti nānāvidhair bhāvair ayodhyendrapurīsamā 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā nāradaḥ ślokaṃ sabhāmadhye puroktavān ।। 

svargaṃ vai sṛjamānasya vyarthaṃ syāt padmajanmanaḥ 
jātāyodhyādhikā svargāt kāmabhogasamanvitā ।। 

tām āvasad ayodhyāṃ tu svabhiṣikto mahīpatiḥ 
jitavān sarvabhūpālān dharmeṇa sa mahābalaḥ ।। 

māṇikyamukuṭair yuktai rājabhir maṇḍalādhipaiḥ 
namadbhir bhaktibhītibhyāṃ pādau tasya kiṇīkṛtau ।। 

ikṣvākur akṣatabalaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ 
tejasendreṇa sadṛśo manoḥ sūnuḥ pratāpavan ।। 

dharmato nyāyataś caiva vedajñair brāhmaṇair yutaḥ 
pālayāmasa dharmātmā āsamudrāṃ mahīm imām ।। 

astrair jigāya sakalān saṃyuge bhūpatīn balī 
avajitya sutīkṣṇais tu tanmaṇḍalam athāharat ।। 

jitavān paralokāṃś ca kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ 
dānaiś ca vividhair brahman rājekṣvākuḥ pratāpavān ।। 

bāhudvayena vasudhāṃ jihvāgreṇa sarasvatīm 
babhāra padmām urasā bhaktiṃ cittena mādhave ।। 

saṃtiṣṭhato hare rūpam upaviṣṭaṃ ca mādhavam 
śayānam apy anantaṃ tu kārayitvā paṭe amalam ।। 

trikālaṃ trayam ārādhya rūpaṃ viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ 
gandhapuṣpādibhir nityaṃ reme dṛṣṭvā paṭe harim ।। 

kṛṣṇaṃ taṃ kṛṣṇameghābhaṃ bhujagendranivāsinam 
padmākṣaṃ pītavāsaṃ ca svapneṣv api sa dṛṣṭavān ।। 

cakāra meghe tadvarṇe bahumānamatiṃ nṛpaḥ 
pakṣapātaṃ ca tannāmni mṛge padme ca tādṛśe ।। 

divyākṛtiṃ hareḥ sākṣād draṣṭuṃ tasya mahībhṛtaḥ 
atīva tṛṣṇā saṃjātā apūrvaiva hi sattama ।। 

tṛṣṇāyāṃ tu prabuddhāyāṃ manasaiva hi pārthivaḥ 
cintayāmasa matimān rājyabhogam asāravat ।। 

veśmadārasutakṣetraṃ saṃyastaṃ yena duḥkhadam 
vairāgyajñānapūrveṇa loke asmin nāsti tatsamaḥ ।। 

ity evaṃ cintayitvā tu tapasy āsaktacetanaḥ 
vasiṣṭhaṃ paripapraccha tatropāyaṃ purohitam ।। 

tapobalena deveśaṃ nārāyaṇam ajaṃ mune 
draṣṭum icchāmy ahaṃ tatra upāyaṃ taṃ vadasva me ।। 

ityuktaḥ prāha rājānāṃ tapasy āsaktamānasam 
vasiṣṭhaḥ sarvadharmajñaḥ sadā tasya hite rataḥ ।। 

yadīcchasi mahārāja draṣṭuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ param 
tapasā sukṛteneha ārādhaya janārdanam ।। 

kenāpy ataptatapasā devadevo janārdanaḥ 
draṣṭuṃ na śakyate jātu tasmāt taṃ tapasārcaya ।। 

pūrvadakṣiṇadigbhāge sarayūtīrage nṛpa 
gālavapramukhānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇām asti cāśramaḥ ।। 

pañcayojanam adhvānaṃ sthānam asmāt tu pāvanam 
nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpuṣpasamākulam ।। 

svamantriṇi mahāprājñe nītimaty arjune nṛpa 
svarājyabhāraṃ vinyasya karmakāṇḍam api dvija ।। 

stutvārādhya gaṇādhyakṣam ito vraja vināyakam 
tapaḥsiddhyartham anvicchaṃs tasmāt tatra tapaḥ kuru ।। 

tāpasaṃ veṣam āsthāya śākamūlaphalāśanaḥ 
dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ devam imaṃ mantraṃ sadā japa ।। 

oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya ।

eṣa siddhikaro mantro dvādaśākṣarasaṃjñitaḥ 
japtvainaṃ munayaḥ siddhiṃ parāṃ prāptāḥ purātanāḥ ।। 

gatvā gatvā nivartante candrasūryādayo grahāḥ 
adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ ।। 

bāhyendriyaṃ hṛdi sthāpya manaḥ sūkṣme parātmani 
nṛpa saṃjapa tan mantraṃ draṣṭavyo madhusūdanaḥ ।। 

iti te kathitopāyo hariprāptes tapaḥkṛtau 
pṛcchataḥ sāṃprataṃ bhūyo yadīcchasi kuruṣva tat ।। 

ity evam ukto muninā sa rājā rājyaṃ bhuvo mantrivare samarpya 
stutvā gaṇeśaṃ sumanobhir arcya gataḥ purāt svāt tapase dhṛtātmā ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ikṣvākucaritraṃ caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

kathaṃ stuto gaṇādhyakṣas tena rājñā mahātmanā 
yathā tena tapas taptaṃ tan me vada mahāmate ।। 

caturthīdivase rājā snātvā triṣavaṇaṃ dvija 
raktāmbaradharo bhūtvā raktagandhānulepanaḥ ।। 

suraktakusumair hṛdyair vināyakam athārcayat 
raktacandanatoyena snānapūrvaṃ yathāvidhi ।। 

vilipya raktagandhena raktapuṣpaiḥ prapūjayat 
tato asau dattavān dhūpam ājyayuktaṃ sacandanam 
naivedyaṃ caiva hāridraṃ guḍakhaṇḍaghṛtaplutam ।। 

evaṃ suvidhinā pūjya vināyakam athāstavīt ।। b

namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ stoṣye aham taṃ vināyakam ।। d

mahāgaṇapatiṃ śūram ajitaṃ jñānavardhanam 
ekadantaṃ dvidantaṃ ca caturdantaṃ caturbhujam ।। 

tryakṣaṃ triśūlahastaṃ ca raktanetraṃ varapradam 
āmbikeyaṃ śūrpakarṇaṃ pracaṇḍaṃ ca vināyakam ।। 

āraktaṃ daṇḍinaṃ caivam vahnivaktraṃ hutapriyam 
anarcito vighnakaraḥ sarvakāryeṣu yo nṛṇām ।। 

taṃ namāmi gaṇādhyakṣaṃ bhīmam ugram umāsutam 
madamattaṃ virūpākṣaṃ bhaktavighnanivārakam ।। 

sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ bhinnāñjanasamaprabham 
baddhaṃ sunirmalaṃ śāntaṃ namasyāmi vināyakam ।। 

namo astu gajavaktrāya gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ 
merumandararūpāya namaḥ kailāsavāsine ।। 

virūpāya namas te astu namas te brahmacāriṇe 
bhaktastutāya devāya namas tubhyaṃ vināyaka ।। 

tvayā purāṇa pūrveṣāṃ devānāṃ kāryasiddhaye 
gajarūpaṃ samāsthāya trāsitāḥ sarvadānavāḥ ।। 

ṛṣīṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca nāyakatvaṃ prakāśitam 
yatas tataḥ surair agre pūjyase tvaṃ bhavātmaja ।। 

tvām ārādhya gaṇādhyakṣaṃ sarvajñaṃ kāmarūpiṇam 
kāryārthaṃ raktakusumai raktacandanavāribhiḥ ।। 

raktāmbaradharo bhūtvā caturthyām arcayej japet 
trikālaṃ ekakālaṃ vā pūjayen niyatāśanaḥ ।। 

rājānaṃ rājaputraṃ vā rājamantriṇam eva vā 
rājyaṃ ca sarvavighneśa vaśaṃ kuryāt sarāṣṭrakam ।। 

avighnaṃ tapaso mahyaṃ kuru naumi vināyaka 
mayetthaṃ saṃstuto bhaktyā pūjitaś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। 

yat phalaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu sarvayajñeṣu yat phalam 
tat phalaṃ pūrṇam āpnoti stutvā devaṃ vināyakam ।। 

viṣamaṃ na bhavet tasya na ca gacchet parābhavam 
na ca vighno bhavet tasya jāto jātismaro bhavet ।। 

ya idaṃ paṭhate stotraṃ ṣaḍbhir māsair varaṃ labhet 
saṃvatsareṇa siddhiṃ ca labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

evaṃ stutvā purā rājā gaṇādhyakṣaṃ dvijottama 
tāpasaṃ veṣam āsthāya tapaś cartum gato vanam ।। 

utsṛjya vastraṃ nāgatvaksadṛśaṃ bahumūlyakam 
kaṭhināṃ tu tvacaṃ vārkṣīṃ kaṭyāṃ dhatte nṛpottamaḥ ।। 

tathā ratnāni divyāni valayāni nirasya tu 
akṣasūtram alaṃkāraṃ phalaiḥ padmasya śobhanam ।। 

tathottamāṅge mukuṭaṃ ratnahāṭakaśobhitam 
tyaktvā jaṭākalāpaṃ tu taporthe bibhṛyān nṛpaḥ ।। 

kṛtvetthaṃ sa tapoveṣaṃ vasiṣṭhoktaṃ tapovanam 
praviśya ca tapas tepe śākamūlaphalāśanaḥ ।। 

grīṣme pañcāgnimadhyastho atapat kāle mahātapāḥ 
varṣākāle nirālambo hemante ca sarojale ।। 

indriyāṇi samastāni niyamya hṛdaye punaḥ 
mano viṣṇau samāveśya mantraṃ vai dvādaśākṣaram ।। 

japato vāyubhakṣasya tasya rājño mahātmanaḥ 
āvir babhūva bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। 

tam āgatam athālokya padmayoniṃ caturmukham 
praṇamya bhaktibhāvena stutyā ca paryatoṣayat ।। 

namo hiraṇyagarbhāya jagatsraṣṭre mahātmane 
vedaśāstrārthaviduṣe caturvaktrāya te namaḥ ।। 

iti stuto jagatsraṣṭā brahmā prāha nṛpottamam ।। b

tapasy abhirataṃ śāntaṃ tyaktarājyaṃ mahāsukham ।। d

lokaprakāśako rājan sūryas tava pitāmahaḥ ।। f

munīnām api sarveṣāṃ sadā mānyo manuḥ pitā 
kṛtavantau tapaḥ pūrvaṃ tīvraṃ pitṛpitāmahau ।। 

kimarthaṃ rājyabhogaṃ tu tyaktvā sarvaṃ nṛpottama 
tapaḥ karoṣi ghoraṃ tvaṃ samācakṣva mahāmate ।। 

ityukto brahmaṇā rājā taṃ praṇamyābravīd vacaḥ 
dṛṣṭum icchaṃs tapaścaryābalena madhusūdanam ।। 

karomy evaṃ tapo brahman śaṅkhacakragadādharam 
ityuktaḥ prāha rājānaṃ padmajanmā hasann iva ।। 

na śakyas tapasā draṣṭuṃ tvayā nārāyaṇo vibhuḥ 
mādṛśair api no dṛśyaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।। 

purātanīṃ puṇyakathāṃ kathayāmi nibodha me 
niśānte pralaye lokān ninīya kamalekṣaṇaḥ ।। 

anantabhogaśayane yoganidrāṃ gato hariḥ 
sanandanādyair munibhiḥ stūyamāno mahāmate ।। 

tasya suptasya nābhau tu mahat padmam ajāyata 
tasmin padme śubhe rājan jāto ahaṃ vedavit purā ।। 

tato bhūtvā tv adhodṛṣṭir dṛṣṭavān kamalekṣaṇam 
anantabhogaparyaṅke bhinnāñjananibhaṃ harim ।। 

atasīkusumābhāsaṃ śayānaṃ pītavāsasam 
divyaratnavicitrāṅgaṃ mukuṭena virājitam ।। 

kundendusadṛśākāram anantaṃ ca mahāmate 
sahasraphaṇamadhyasthair maṇibhir dīptimattaram ।। 

kṣaṇamātraṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā punas tatra na dṛṣṭavān 
duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo babhūvāhaṃ nṛpottama ।। 

tato nv avātaraṃ tasmāt padmanālaṃ samāśritaḥ 
kautūhalena taṃ draṣṭuṃ nārāyaṇam anāmayam ।। 

tatas tv anviṣya rājendra salilānte na dṛṣṭavān 
śrīśaṃ punas tam evāhaṃ padmam āśritya cintayan ।। 

tad rūpaṃ vāsudevasya draṣṭuṃ tepe mahat tapaḥ 
tato mām antarikṣasthā vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।। 

vṛthā kiṃ kliśyate brahman sāṃprataṃ kuru me vacaḥ 
na dṛśyo bhagavān viṣṇus tapasā mahatāpi te ।। 

sṛṣṭiṃ kuru tadājñapto yadi draṣṭum ihecchasi 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśanāgaparyaṅkaśāyinam ।। 

yad dṛṣṭaṃ śārṅgiṇo rūpaṃ bhinnāñjanasamaprabham 
pratibhāniyataṃ rūpaṃ vimānasthaṃ mahāmate ।। 

bhaja nityam anālasyas tato drakṣyasi mādhavam 
tayetthaṃ codito rājaṃs tyaktvā taptam anukṣaṇam ।। 

sṛṣṭavān lokabhūtānāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ sṛṣṭvā sthitasya ca 
āvir babhūva manasi viśvakarmā prajāpatiḥ ।। 

anantakṛṣṇayos tena dve rūpe nirmite śubhe 
vimānastho yathāpūrvaṃ mayā dṛṣṭo jale nṛpa ।। 

tathaiva taṃ tato bhaktyā saṃpūjyāhaṃ hariṃ sthitaḥ 
tatprasādāt tapaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ mayā jñānam anuttamam ।। 

labdhvā muktiṃ ca paśyāmi avikārakriyāsukham 
tad ahaṃ te pravakṣyāmi hitaṃ nṛpavareśvara ।। 

visṛjyaitat tapo ghoraṃ purīṃ vraja nijāṃ nṛpa 
prajānāṃ pālanaṃ dharmas tapaś caiva mahībhṛtām ।। 

vimānaṃ preṣayiṣyāmi siddhadvijagaṇānvitam 
tatrārādhaya deveśaṃ bāhyārthair akhilaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। 

nārāyaṇam anantākhye śayānaṃ kratubhir yajan 
niṣkāmo nṛpaśārdūla prajā dharmeṇa pālaya ।। 

prasādād vāsudevasya muktis te bhavitā nṛpa 
ity uktvā taṃ jagāmātha brahmalokaṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। 

ikṣvākuś cintayann āste padmayonivaco dvija 
āvir babhūva purato vimānaṃ tan mahībhṛtaḥ ।। 

brahmadattaṃ dvijayutaṃ mādhavānantayoḥ śubham 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā parayā bhaktyā natvā ca puruṣottamam ।। 

ṛṣīn praṇamya viprāṃś ca tad ādāya yayau purīm 
paurair janaiś ca nārībhir dṛṣṭaḥ śobhāsamanvitaiḥ ।। 

lājā vinikṣipadbhiś ca nīto rājā svakaṃ gṛham 
svamandire viśāle tu vimānaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ śubham ।। 

saṃsthāpyārādhayāmasa tair dvijair arcitaṃ harim 
mahiṣyaḥ śobhanā yās tu piṣṭvā tu haricandanam ।। 

mālāṃ kṛtvā sugandhāḍhyāṃ prītis tasya vavardha ha 
paurāḥ karpūraṃ śrīkhaṇḍaṃ kuṅkumādy aguruṃ tathā ।। 

kṛtsnaṃ viśeṣato vastraṃ mahiṣākhyaṃ ca guggulam 
puṣpāṇi viṣṇuyogyāni dadur ānīya bhūpateḥ ।। 

vimānasthaṃ hariṃ pūjya gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt 
trisaṃdhyaṃ parayā bhaktyā japaiḥ stotraiś ca vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।। 

gītaiḥ kolāhalaiḥ śabdaiḥ śaṅkhavāditranāditaiḥ 
prekṣaṇair api śāstroktaiḥ prītaiś ca niśi jāgaraiḥ ।। 

kārayāmasa suciram utsavaṃ paramaṃ hareḥ 
yāgaiś ca toṣayitvā taṃ sarvadevamayaṃ harim ।। 

niṣkāmo dānadharmaiś ca paraṃ jñānam avāptavān 
yajan yajñaṃ mahīṃ rakṣan sa kurvan keśavārcanam ।। 

utpādya putrān pitrarthaṃ dhyānāt tyaktvā kalevaram 
dhyāyan vai kevalaṃ brahma prāptavān vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।। 

ajaṃ viśokaṃ vimalaṃ viśuddhaṃ śāntaṃ sadānandacidātmakaṃ tataḥ 
vihāya saṃsāram anantaduḥkhaṃ jagāma tad viṣṇupadaṃ hi rājā ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ikṣvākucarite pañcaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

ikṣvākor vikukṣināmaputraḥ । 

sa tu siddhe pitari maharṣibhir abhiṣikto dharmeṇa pṛthivīṃ pālayan vimānastham anantabhogaśāyinam acyutam ārādhya yāgair api devān iṣṭvā svaputraṃ rājye subāhum abhiṣicya divam āruroha । subāhor bhrājamānād udyoto abhigīyate । sa tu saptadvīpāṃ pṛthvīṃ dharmeṇa pālayitvā bhaktiṃ parāṃ nārāyaṇe pitāmahavat kṛtvā kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇair yajñeśvaraṃ niṣkāmena manaseṣṭvā nityaṃ nirañjanaṃ nirvikalpaṃ paraṃ jyotir amṛtākṣaraṃ paramātmarūpaṃ dhyātvā harim anantaṃ ca param ārādhya svargalokaṃ gataḥ ।। tasya yuvanāśvo yuvanāśvasya ca māndhātā putro abhavat । sa cābhiṣikto maharṣibhir nisargād eva viṣṇubhakto anantaśayanam acyutaṃ bhaktyārādhayan yāgaiś ca vividhair iṣṭvā saptadvīpavatīṃ pṛthivīṃ paripālya divaṃ gataḥ ।। 

yasyaiṣa śloko gīyate ।

yāvat sūrya udeti sma yāvac ca pratitiṣṭhati 
sarvaṃ tad yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate ।। 

tasya purukuśyo abhavad yena devā brāhmaṇāś ca yāgadānaiḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ ।। 

purukuśyād dṛṣado dṛṣadād abhiśaṃbhuḥ । abhiśaṃbhor dāruṇo dāruṇāt sagaraḥ ।। 

sagarād dharyaśvo haryaśvād dhārīto hārītād rohitāśvaḥ । rohitāśvād aṃśumān ।। 

aṃśumato bhagīrathaḥ । 
ḥyena mahatā tapasā purā divo gaṅgā aśeṣakalmaṣanāśinī caturvidhapuruṣārthadāyinī bhuvam ānītā ।
ḥasthiśarkarābhūtāḥ kapilamaharṣinirdagdhāś ca guravaḥ sagarākhyā gaṅgātoyasaṃspṛṣṭā divam āropitāḥ ।
ḥbhagīrathāt saudāsaḥ saudāsāt satrasavaḥ ।। 
satrasavād anaraṇyo anaraṇyād dīrghabāhuḥ ।। 

dīrghabāhor ajo ajād daśarathaḥ । tasya gṛhe rāvaṇavināśārthaṃ sākṣān nārāyaṇo avatīrṇo rāmaḥ ।। 

ḥsa tu pitṛvacanād bhrātṛbhāryāsahito daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ prāpya tapaś cacāra ।
ḥvane rāvaṇāpahṛtabhāryo bhrātrā saha duḥkhito anekakoṭivānaranāyakasugrīvasahāyo mahodadhau setuṃ nibadhya tair gatvā laṅkāṃ rāvaṇaṃ devakaṇṭakaṃ sabāndhavaṃ hatvā sītām ādāya punar ayodhyāṃ prāpya bharatābhiṣikto vibhīṣaṇāya laṅkārājyaṃ vimānaṃ vā dattvā taṃ preṣayāmasa ।
ḥsa tu parameśvaro vimānastho vibhīṣaṇena nīyamāno laṅkāyām api rākṣasapuryāṃ vastum anicchan puṇyāraṇyaṃ tatra sthāpitavān ।। 

tan nirīkṣya tatraiva mahāhibhogaśayane bhagavān śete । so api vibhīṣaṇas tatas tadvimānaṃ netum asamarthaḥ tadvacanāt svāṃ purīṃ jagāma ।। 

nārāyaṇasaṃnidhānān mahad vaiṣṇavaṃ kṣetram abhavad adyāpi dṛśyate ।

ḥrāmāl lavo lavāt padmaḥ padmād ṛtuparṇa ṛṭuparṇād astrapāṇiḥ ।
ḥastrapāṇeḥ śuddhodanaḥ śuddhodanād buddhaḥ ।
ḥbuddhād vaṃśo nivartate ।। 

ete mahīpā ravivaṃśajās tava prādhānyatas te kathitā mahābalāḥ 
purātanair yair vasudhā prapālitā yajñakriyābhiś ca divaukasair nṛpaiḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sūryavaṃśānucaritaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

atha somavaṃśodbhavānāṃ bhūbhujāṃ saṃkṣepeṇa caritam ucyate ।। 

ādau tāvat samastaṃ trailokyaṃ kukṣau kṛtvā ekārṇave mahāmbhasi nāgabhogaśayane ।। 

ḥṛṅmayo yajurmayaḥ sāmamayo atharvamayo bhagavān nārāyaṇo yoganidrāṃ samārebhe ।
ḥtasya suptasya nābhau mahāpadmam ajāyata ।
ḥtasmin padme caturmukho brahmābhavat ।। 

ḥtasya brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putro atrir abhavat ।
ḥatrer anasūyāyāṃ somaḥ ।
ḥsa tu prajāpater dakṣasya trayastriṃśat kanyā rohiṇyādyā bhāryārthaṃ gṛhītvā priyāyāṃ jyeṣṭhāyāṃ viśeṣāt prasannamanāḥ rohiṇyāṃ budhaṃ putram utpādayāmasa ।। 

ḥbudho api sarvaśāstrajñaḥ pratiṣṭhāne pure avasat ।
ḥilāyāṃ purūravasaṃ putram utpādayāmasa ।
ḥtasyātiśayarūpānvitasya svargabhogān vihāya urvaśī bahukālaṃ bhāryā babhūva ।। 

purūravasaḥ urvaśyām āyuḥ putro jajñe । sa tu rājyaṃ dharmataḥ kṛtvā divam āruroha ।। 

ḥāyo rūpavatyāṃ nahuṣaḥ putro abhavat ।
ḥyenendratvaṃ prāptam ।
ḥnahuṣasyāpi pitṛmatyāṃ yayātiḥ ।। 

yasya vaṃśajā vṛṣṇayaḥ । yayāteḥ śarmiṣṭhāyāṃ pūrur abhavat ।। 

pūror vaṃśadāyāṃ saṃyātiḥ putro abhavat । yasya pṛthivyāṃ saṃpannāḥ sarve kāmāḥ ।। 

saṃyāter bhānudattāyāṃ sārvabhaumaḥ । sa tu sarvāṃ pṛthivīṃ dharmeṇa paripālayan narasiṃhaṃ bhagavantam ārādhya yāgadānaiḥ siddhim āpa ।। 

tasya sārvabhaumasya vaidehyāṃ bhojaḥ । yasya vaṃśe purā devāsurasaṃgrāme viṣṇucakrahataḥ kālanemiḥ kaṃso bhūtvā vṛṣṇivaṃśajena vāsudevena ghātito nidhanaṃ gataḥ ।। 

ḥtasya bhojasya kaliṅgāyāṃ duṣyantaḥ ।
ḥsa tu narasiṃhaṃ bhagavantam ārādhya tatprasādān niṣkaṇṭakaṃ rājyaṃ dharmeṇa kṛtvā divaṃ prāptavān ।
ḥduṣyantasya śakuntalāyāṃ bharataḥ sa tu dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kurvan kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ sarvadevatāmayaṃ bhagavantam ārādhya nivṛttādhikāro brahmadhyānaparo vaiṣṇave pare jyotiṣi layam avāpa ।। 

bharatasya ānandāyām ajamīḍhaḥ । sa ca paramavaiṣṇavo narasiṃham ārādhya jātaputro dharmeṇa kṛtarājyo viṣṇupuram āruroha ।। 

ḥajamīḍhasya sudevyāṃ vṛṣṇiḥ putro abhavat ।
ḥso api bahuvarṣaṃ dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kurvan duṣṭanigrahaṃ śiṣṭaparipālanaṃ saptadvīpāṃ vaśe cakre ।
ḥvṛṣṇer ugrasenāyāṃ pratyañcaḥ putro babhūva ।। 

ḥso api dharmeṇa medinīṃ pālayan pratisaṃvatsaraṃ jyotiṣṭomaṃ cakāra ।
ḥnirvāṇam api labdhavān ।
ḥpratyañcasya bahurūpāyāṃ śāṃtanuḥ ।। 

tasya devadattasyandanārohaṇam aśakyaṃ babhūva purataḥ śakyaṃ ca ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe somavaṃśavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

syandanārohaṇe pūrvam aśaktiḥ śāṃtanoḥ katham 
paścāc chaktiḥ kathaṃ cāsīt tasya vai tad vadasva naḥ ।। 

bharadvāja śṛṇuṣvaitat purāvṛttaṃ vadāmi te 
sarvapāpaharaṃ tad dhi caritaṃ śāṃtanor nṛṇām ।। 

babhūva śāṃtanur bhakto narasiṃhatanau purā 
nāradoktavidhānena pūjayāmasa mādhavam ।। 

narasiṃhasya devasya nirmālyaṃ tena laṅghitam 
rājñā śāṃtanunā vipra tasmāt syandanam uttamam ।। 

devadattaṃ tad āroḍhum aśaktas tatkṣaṇād abhūt 
kim iyaṃ me gatir bhagnā sahasā vai rathāt tataḥ ।। 

duḥkhaṃ cintayatas tasya saṃprāpto nāradaḥ kila 
kiṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ sthito rājann iti pṛṣṭaḥ sa śāṃtanuḥ ।। 

nāradaitan na jānāmi gatibhaṅgasya kāraṇam 
ityukto nārado dhyātvā jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। 

śāṃtanuṃ prāha rājānaṃ vinayena yataḥ sthitaḥ 
yatra kvāpi tvayā rājan narasiṃhasya vai dhruvam ।। 

nirmālyo laṅghitas tasmād rathārohaṇakarmaṇi 
gatir bhagnā mahārāja śrūyatām atra kāraṇam ।। 

antarvedyāṃ purā rājann āsīt kaścin mahāmatiḥ 
mālākāro ravir nāmnā tena vṛndāvanaṃ kṛtam ।। 

vividhāni ca puṣpārthaṃ vanāni sukṛtāni vai 
mallikāmālatījātibakulādīni sarvaśaḥ ।। 

prākāram ucchritaṃ tasya svabhūmau cāpi vistṛtam 
alaṅghyam apraveśyaṃ ca kṛtvā cakre svakaṃ gṛham ।। 

gṛhaṃ praviśya taddvāraṃ bhaven nānyatra sattama 
evaṃ kṛtvā nu vasato mālākārasya dhīmataḥ ।। 

puṣpitaṃ tad vanaṃ tv āsīd gandhāmoditadiṅmukham 
bhāryayā saha puṣpāṇi samāhṛtya dine dine ।। 

kṛtvā mālāṃ yathānyāyaṃ narasiṃhasya nityaśaḥ 
dadau kāścid dvijebhyaś ca kāścid vikrīya poṣaṇam ।। 

cakre samāt prajīvī ca bhāryāder ātmanas tathā 
atha svargād upāgamya indraputro rathena vai ।। 

apsarogaṇasaṃyukto niśi puṣpāṇi saṃharet 
tadgandhalipsuḥ sarvāṇi vicityāhṛtya gacchati ।। 

dine dine hṛte puṣpe mālākāro apy acintayat 
nānyad dvāraṃ vanasyāsyālaṅghyaprākāram unnatam ।। 

samastapuṣpajātasya haraṇe niśi vai nṛṇām 
ahaṃ śaktiṃ na paśyāmi kim idaṃ nu parīkṣaye ।। 

iti saṃcintya medhāvī jāgrad rātrau vane sthitaḥ 
tathaivāgatya puṣpāṇi saṃgṛhītva gataḥ pumān ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā duḥkhito atīva mālyajīvī vane abhavat 
tato nidrāṃ gataḥ svapne dṛṣṭavāṃs taṃ nṛkesarim ।। 

tadvākyaṃ śrutavāṃś caivaṃ nirmālyaṃ mama putraka 
ānīya kṣipyatāṃ kṣipraṃ puṣpārāmasamīpataḥ ।। 

indraputrasya duṣṭasya nānyad asti nivāraṇam 
iti śrutvā harer vākyaṃ narasiṃhasya dhīmataḥ ।। 

buddhvānīya tu nirmālyaṃ tathā cakre yathoditam 
so apy āgatya yathāpūrvaṃ rathenālakṣitena tu ।। 

rathād uttīrya puṣpāṇi vicinvaṃs tadbhuvi sthitam 
nirmālyaṃ laṅghayāmasa indrasūnur aniṣṭakṛt ।। 

tatas tasya na śaktiḥ syad rathārohaṇakarmaṇi 
uktaḥ sārathinā caiva rathasyārohaṇe tava ।। 

narasiṃhasya nirmālyalaṅghane nāsti yogyatā 
gacchāmi divam evāhaṃ tvaṃ bhūmyāṃ vasa māruha ।। 

tenaivam ukto matimāṃs tam āha harinandanaḥ 
pāpasya nodanaṃ tv atra karmaṇā yena me bhavet ।। 

tad uktvā gaccha nākaṃ tvaṃ karmāsmān sārathe drutam ।। b

rāmasattre kurukṣetre dvādaśābde tu nityaśaḥ ।। d

dvijocchiṣṭāpanayanaṃ kṛtvā tvaṃ śuddhim eṣyasi 
ity uktvāsau gataḥ svargaṃ sārathir devasevitam ।। 

indrasūnuḥ kurukṣetraṃ prāptaḥ sārasvataṃ taṭam 
rāmasattre tathā kuryād dvijocchiṣṭasya mārjanam ।। 

pūrṇe dvādaśame varṣe tam ūcuḥ śaṅkitā dvijāḥ 
kas tvaṃ brūhi mahābhāga nityam ucchiṣṭamārjakaḥ ।। 

na bhuñjase ca naḥ sattre śaṅkā no mahatī bhavet 
ityuktaḥ kathayitvā tu yathāvṛttam anukramāt ।। 

jagāma tridivaṃ kṣipraṃ rathena tanayo hareḥ 
tasmāt tvam api bhūpāla brāhmaṇocchiṣṭam ādarāt ।। 

mārjanaṃ kuru rāmasya sattre dvādaśavārṣike 
brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paraṃ nāsti sarvapāpaharaṃ param ।। 

evaṃ kṛte devadattasyandanārohaṇe gatiḥ 
bhaviṣyati mahīpāla prāyaścitte kṛte tava ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ mā laṅghaya mahāmate 
narasiṃhasya devasya tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām ।। 

ityuktaḥ śāṃtanus tena brāhmaṇocchiṣṭamārjanam 
kṛtavān dvādaśābdaṃ tu āruroha rathaṃ ca tam ।। 

evaṃ purvam aśaktiḥ syād rathārohe mahīkṣitaḥ 
paścāt tasyaiva viprendra śaktir evam ajāyata ।। 

evaṃ te kathito vipra doṣo nirmālyalaṅghane 
puṇyaṃ tathā dvijānāṃ tu proktam ucchiṣṭamārjane ।। 

bhaktyā dvijocchiṣṭam ihāpamārjayec chucir naro yaḥ susamāhitātmā 
sa pāpabandhaṃ pravihāya bhuṅkte gavāṃ pradānasya phalaṃ divi sthitaḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe śāṃtanucaritaṃ nāmāṣṭaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

śaṃtanayor yojanagandhāyāṃ vicitravīryaḥ । sa tu hastināpure sthitvā prajāḥ svadharmeṇa pālayan devāṃś ca yāgaiḥ pitṛṃś ca śrāddhaiḥ saṃtarpya saṃjātaputro divam āruroha ।। 

ḥvicitravīryasyāmbālikāyāṃ pāṇḍuḥ putro jajñe ।
ḥso api rājyaṃ dharmataḥ kṛtvā muniśāpāc charīraṃ vihāya devalokam avāpa ।
ḥtasya pāṇḍoḥ kuntidevyām arjunaḥ ।। 

sa tu mahatā tapasā śaṃkaraṃ toṣayitvā pāśupatam astram avāpya triviṣṭapādhipateḥ śatrūn nivātakavacān dānavān hatvā khāṇḍavavanam agner yathāruci nivedya tṛptāgnito divyān varān avāpya suyodhanena hṛtarājyo dharmabhīmanakulasahadevadraupadīsahito virāṭanagare ajñātavāsaṃ caritvā gograhe ca bhīṣmadroṇakṛpaduryodhanakarṇādīn jitvā samastagomaṇḍalaṃ nivartayitvā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha virāṭarājakṛtapūjo vāsudevasahitaḥ kurukṣetre dhārtarāṣṭrair bahubalair yuddhaṃ kurvan bhīṣmadroṇakṛpaśalyakarṇādibhir bhūriparākramaiḥ kṣatriyair nānādeśāgatair anekair api rājaputraiḥ saha duryodhanādīn dhārtarāṣṭrān hatvā svarājyaṃ prāpya dharmeṇa rājyaṃ paripālya bhrātṛbhiḥ saha mudito divam āruroha ।। 

arjunasya subhadrāyām abhimanyuḥ । yena bhāratayuddhe cakravyūhaṃ praviśyānekabhūbhujo nidhanaṃ prāpitāḥ ।। 

abhimanyor uttarāyāṃ parīkṣitaḥ । so apy abhiṣikto vanaṃ gacchatā dharmaputreṇa rājyaṃ kṛtvā rājaputro nākaṃ saṃprāpya reme ।। 

parīkṣitān mātṛvatyāṃ janamejayaḥ । yena brahmahatyāvāraṇārthaṃ mahābhārataṃ vyāsaśiṣyād vaiśaṃpāyanāt sādyantaṃ śrutam ।। 

rājyaṃ ca dharmataḥ kṛtvā divam āruroha । janamejayasya puṣpavatyāṃ śatānīkaḥ ।। 

sa tu dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kurvan saṃsāraduḥkhād viraktaḥ śaunakopadeśena kriyāyogena sakalalokanāthaṃ viṣṇum ārādhya niṣkāmo vaiṣṇavaṃ padam avāpa । tasya śatānīkasya phalavatyāṃ sahasrānīkaḥ ।। 

sa tu bāla evābhiṣikto narasiṃhe atyantaṃ bhaktimān abhavat । tasya caritam upariṣṭād bhaviṣyati ।। 

sahasrānīkasya mṛgavantyām udayanaḥ । so api rājyaṃ kṛtvā dharmato nārāyaṇam ārādhya tatpuram avāpa ।। 

ḥudayanasya vāsavadattāyāṃ naravāhanaḥ ।
ḥsa tu yathānyāyaṃ rājyaṃ kṛtvā divam avāpa ।
ḥnaravāhanasyāśvamedhadattāyāṃ kṣemakaḥ ।। 

sa ca rājyasthaḥ prajāḥ paripālya mlecchābhibhūte jagati jñānabalāt kalāpagrāmam āśritaḥ ।। 

yaḥ śraddadhānaḥ paṭhate śṛṇoti vā harau ca bhaktiṃ caritaṃ mahībhṛtām 
sa saṃtatiṃ prāpya viśuddhakarmakṛd divaṃ samāsādya vasec ciraṃ sukhī ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe śaṃtanusaṃtativarṇanaṃ nāma ekonatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūgolaṃ dvijasattamāḥ 
saṃkṣepāt parvatākīrṇaṃ nadībhiś ca samantataḥ ।। 

ḥjambuplakṣaśālmalakuśakrauñcaśākapuṣkarasaṃjñāḥ sapta dvīpāḥ ।
ḥlakṣayojanapramāṇāj jambudvīpād uttarottaradviguṇāḥ ।
ḥlavaṇekṣurasasurāsarpirdadhidugdhasvacchodakasaṃjñaiḥ parasparaṃ dviguṇaiḥ saptasamudrair valayākārais te dvīpāḥ paridhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। 

yo asau manuputraḥ priyavrato nāma sa saptadvīpādhipatir babhūva । tasya agnīdhrādayo daśa putrā babhūvuḥ ।। 

ḥtrayaḥ pravrajitāḥ ।
ḥśiṣṭānāṃ saptānāṃ saptadvīpāḥ pitrā dattāḥ ।
ḥtatra jambudvīpādhipater agnīdhrasya nava putrāḥ jātāḥ ।। 

nābhiḥ kiṃpuruṣaś caiva harivarṣa ilāvṛtaḥ 
ramyo hiraṇyayaś caiva kurur bhadraś ca ketumān ।। 

ḥnavavarṣāḥ vibhajya putrebhyaḥ pitrā dattā vanaṃ praviśatā ।
ḥagnīdhrīyaṃ himāhvayam ।
ḥyasyādhipatir nābheḥ ṛṣabhaḥ putro babhūva ।। 

ṛṣabhād bharato bharatena cirakālaṃ dharmeṇa pālitatvād idaṃ bhārataṃ varṣam abhūt । 
ḥilāvṛtasya madhye meruḥ suvarṇamayaś caturaśītisahasrāṇi yojanāni tasyocchrāyaḥ ।
ḥṣoḍaśasahasram apy adhastād avagāḍhaḥ ।
ḥtaddviguṇo mūrdhni vistāraḥ ।। 
tanmadhye brahmaṇaḥ purī । aindryām indrasya cāmarāvatī । āgneyyām agnes tejovatī । yāmyāṃ yamasya saṃyamanī । nairṛtyāṃ nirṛter bhayaṃkarī । vāruṇyāṃ varuṇasya viśvāvatī । 
ḥvāyavyāṃ vāyor gandhavatī ।
ḥudīcyāṃ somasya vibhāvarīti ।
ḥnavavarṣānvitaṃ jambūdvīpaṃ puṇyaparvataiḥ puṇyanadībhir anvitam ।। 
kiṃpuruṣādīny aṣṭavarṣāṇi puṇyavatāṃ bhogasthānāni sākṣād bhāratavarṣam ekaṃ karmabhūmiś cāturvarṇyayutam ।। 

tatraiva karmabhiḥ svargaṃ kṛteḥ prāpsyanti mānavāḥ 
muktiś cātraiva niṣkāmaiḥ prāpyate jñānakarmabhiḥ 
adhogatim ito vipra yānti vai pāpakāriṇaḥ ।। 

ye pāpakāriṇas tān viddhi pātālatale narake koṭisamanvitān ।। 

ḥatha sapta kulaparvatāḥ kathyante ।
ḥmahendro malayaḥ śuktimān ṛṣyamūkaḥ sahyaparvato vindhyaḥ pāriyātraḥ ।
ḥity ete bhārate kulaparvatāḥ ।। 

narmadā surasā ṛṣikulyā bhīmarathī kṛṣṇāveṇī candrabhāgā tāmraparṇī ity etāḥ sapta nadyaḥ । gaṅgā yamunā godāvarī tuṅgabhadrā kāverī sarayūr ity etā mahānadyaḥ papaghnyaḥ ।। 

jambunāmnā ca vikhyātaṃ jambudvīpam idaṃ śubham 
lakṣayojanavistīrṇam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tu bhāratam ।। 

ḥṛkṣadvīpādipuṇyā janapadāḥ ।
ḥniṣkāmā ye svadharmeṇa narasiṃhaṃ yajanti te tatra nivasanti ।
ḥadhikārakṣayān muktiṃ ca prāpnuvanti ।। 

ḥjambvādyāḥ svādūdakāntāḥ sapta payodhayaḥ ।
ḥtataḥ parā hiraṇmayī bhūmiḥ ।
ḥtato lokālokaparvataḥ eṣa bhūrlokaḥ ।। 

asyopari antarikṣalokaḥ । khecarāṇāṃ ramyas tadūrdhvaṃ svargalokaḥ ।। 

svargasthānaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ procyamānaṃ nibodhata 
bhārate kṛtapuṇyānāṃ devānām api cālayam ।। 

madhye pṛthivyām adrīndro bhāsvān merur hiraṇmayaḥ 
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi caturāśītim ucchritaḥ ।। 

praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastād dharaṇyāṃ dharaṇīdharaḥ 
tāvatpramāṇā pṛthivī parvatasya samantataḥ ।। 

tasya śṛṅgatrayaṃ mūrdhni svargo yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpuṣpopaśobhitam ।। 

madhyamaṃ paścimaṃ pūrvaṃ meroḥ śṛṅgāṇi trīṇi vai 
madhyamaṃ sphāṭikaṃ śṛṅgaṃ vaiḍūryamaṇikāmayam ।। 

indranīlamayaṃ pūrvaṃ māṇikyaṃ paścimaṃ smṛtam 
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi niyutāni caturdaśa ।। 

ucchritaṃ madhyamaṃ śṛṅgaṃ svargo yatra triviṣṭapaḥ 
aprabhāntaritaṃ śṛṅgaṃ mūrdhni chatrākṛti sthitam ।। 

pūrvam uttaraśṛṅgāṇām antaraṃ madhyamasya ca 
triviṣṭapo nākapṛṣṭhe hy apsarāḥ santi nirvṛtāḥ ।। 

ānando atha pramodaś ca svargaśṛṅge tu madhyame 
śvetaś ca pauṣṭikaś caiva upaśobhanamanmathau ।। 

āhlādaḥ svargarājā vai svargaśṛṅge tu paścime 
nirmamo nirahaṃkāraḥ saubhāgyaś cātinirmalaḥ ।। 

svargāś caiva dvijaśreṣṭha pūrvaśṛṅge samāsthitaḥ 
ekaviṃśāni svargā vai niviṣṭā merumūrdhani ।। 

ahiṃsādānakartāro yajñānaṃ tapasāṃ tathā 
tat teṣu nivasanti sma janāḥ krodhavivarjitāḥ ।। 

jalapraveśe cānandaṃ pramodaṃ vahnisāhase 
bhṛguprapāte saukhyaṃ ca raṇaṃ caivāsya nirmalam ।। 

anāśake tu saṃnyāse mṛto gacchet triviṣṭapam 
ṛtuyājī nākapṛṣṭhaṃ agnihotrī ca nirvṛtim ।। 

taḍāgakūpakartā ca labhate pauṣṭikaṃ dvijaḥ 
suvarṇadāyī saubhāgyaṃ labhan svargaṃ tapaḥ phalam ।। 

śītakāle mahāvahniṃ prajvālayati yo naraḥ 
sarvasattvahitārthāya svargaṃ so apsarasaṃ labhet ।। 

hiraṇyagopradāne hi nirahaṃkāram āpnuyāt 
bhūmidānena śuddhena labhate śāntikaṃ padam ।। 

raupyadānena svargaṃ tu nirmalaṃ labhate naraḥ 
aśvadānena puṇyāhaṃ kanyādānena maṅgalam ।। 

dvijebhyas tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā dattvā vastrāṇi bhaktitaḥ 
śvetaṃ tu labhate svargaṃ yatra gatvā na śocate ।। 

kapilāgopradānena paramārthe mahīyate 
govṛṣasya pradānena svargaṃ manmathām āpnuyāt ।। 

māghamāse saritsnāyī tiladhenupradas tathā 
chatropānahadātā ca svargaṃ yāty upaśobhanam ।। 

devatāyatanaṃ kṛtvā dvijaśuśrūṣakas tathā 
tīrthayātrāparaś caiva svargarāje mahīyate ।। 

ekānnabhogī yo martyo naktabhogī ca nityaśaḥ 
upavāsī trirātrādyaiḥ śāntaḥ svargaṃ śubhaṃ labhet ।। 

saritsnāyī jitakrodho brahmacārī dṛḍhavrataḥ 
nirmalaṃ svargam āpnoti yathābhūtahite rataḥ 
vidyādānena medhāvī nirahaṃkāram āpnuyāt ।। 

yena yena hi bhāvena yad yad dānaṃ prayacchati 
tat tat svargam avāpnoti yad yad icchati mānavaḥ ।। 

catvāri atidānāni kanyā gaur bhūḥ sarasvatī 
narakād uddharanty ete jayavāhanadohanāt ।। 

yas tu sarvāṇi dānāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati 
saṃprāpya na nivarteta svargaṃ śāntam anāmayam ।। 

śṛṅge tu paścime yatra brahmā tatra sthitaḥ svayam 
pūrvaśṛṅge svayaṃ viṣṇuḥ madhye caiva śivaḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

ataḥ paraṃ tu viprendra svargādhvānam imaṃ śṛṇu 
vimalaṃ vipulaṃ buddham upary upari saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

prathame tu kumāras tu dvitīye mātaraḥ sthitaḥ 
tṛtīye siddhagandharvās turye vidyādharā dvija ।। 

pañcame nāgarājā ca ṣaṣṭhe tu vinatāsutaḥ 
saptame divyapitaro dharmarājas tathāṣṭame 
navame tu tathā dakṣa ādityo daśame pathi ।। 

bhūrlokāc chatasahasrād ūrdhvaṃ carati bhāskaraḥ 
yojanānāṃ sahasre dve viṣṭambhanasamaṃ tataḥ ।। 

triguṇaṃ pariṇāhena sūryabimbaṃ pramāṇataḥ 
somapuryāṃ vibhāvaryāṃ madhyāhne cāryamā yadā 
mahendrasyāmarāvatyāṃ tadā tiṣṭhati bhāskaraḥ ।। 

madhyāhne tv amarāvatyāṃ yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ 
tadā saṃyamane yāmye tatrodyaṃs tu pradṛśyate ।। 

meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kurvan bhāty eva savitā sadā 
dhruvādhāras tathottiṣṭhan vālikhilyādibhiḥ stutaḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe bhūgolakathane triṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

ko asau dhruvaḥ kasya sutaḥ sūryādhāro abhavat katham 
vicintya kathayāśu tvaṃ sūta jīva samāḥ śatam ।। 

manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyāsīd uttānacaraṇaḥ sutaḥ 
tasya kṣitipater vipra dvau sutau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। 

surucyām uttamo jyeṣṭhaḥ sunītyāṃ tu dhruvo aparaḥ 
madhyesabhaṃ narapater upaviṣṭasya caikadā ।। 

sunītyā rājasevāyai niyukto alaṃkṛtaḥ sutaḥ 
dhruvo dhātreyikāputraiḥ samaṃ vinayatatparaḥ ।। 

sa gatvottānacaraṇaṃ kṣoṇīśaṃ praṇanāma ha 
dṛṣṭvottamaṃ tadutsaṅge niviṣṭaṃ janakasya vai ।। 

prāpya siṃhāsanasthaṃ ca nṛpatiṃ bālacāpalāt 
ārurukṣum avekṣyāmuṃ surucir dhruvam abravīt ।। 

daurbhageya kim āroḍhum iccher aṅkaṃ mahīpateḥ 
bāla bāliśabuddhitvād abhāgyājāṭharodbhavaḥ ।। 

asmin siṃhāsane sthātuṃ sukṛtaṃ kiṃ tvayā kṛtam ।। 

yadi syāt sukṛtaṃ tat kiṃ durbhāgyodarago abhavaḥ 
anenaivānumānena budhyasva svalpapuṇyatām ।। 

bhūtvā rājakumāro api nālaṃkuryā mamodaram 
sukukṣijaṃ amuṃ paśya tvam uttamam anuttamam ।। 

adhijānu dharājaner mānena paribṛṃhitam ।। b

madhyerājasabhaṃ bālas tayeti paribhartsitaḥ ।। d

nipatannetrabāṣpāmbur dhairyāt kiṃcin na coktavān 
ucitaṃ nocitaṃ kiṃcin nocivān so api pārthivaḥ ।। 

niyantrito mahiṣyāś ca tasyāḥ saubhāgyagauravāt 
visarjitasabhālokaṃ śokaṃ saṃhṛtya ceṣṭitaiḥ ।। 

śaiśavaiḥ sa śiśur natvā nṛpaṃ svasadanaṃ yayau 
sunītir nītinilayam avalokyātha bālakam ।। 

mukhalakṣmyaiva cājñāsīd dhruvaṃ rājāpamānitam 
atha dṛṣṭvā sunītiṃ tu raho antaḥpuravāsinīm ।। 

āliṅgya dīrghaṃ niḥśvasya muktakaṇṭhaṃ ruroda ha 
sāntvayitvā sunītis taṃ vadanaṃ parimārjya ca ।। 

dukūlāñcalasaṃparkair vījya taṃ mṛdupāṇinā 
papraccha tanayaṃ mātā vada rodanakāraṇam ।। 

vidyamāne narapatau śiśo kenāpamānitaḥ ।। b

saṃpṛcche janani tvāhaṃ saṃyak śaṃsa mamāgrataḥ ।। d

bhāryātve api ca sāmānye kathaṃ sā suruciḥ priyā 
kathaṃ na bhavatī mātaḥ priyā kṣitipater asi ।। 

katham uttamatāṃ prāpta uttamaḥ suruceḥ sutaḥ 
kumāratve api sāmānye kathaṃ cāham anuttamaḥ ।। 

kathaṃ tvaṃ mandabhāgyāsi sukukṣiḥ suruciḥ katham 
kathaṃ nṛpāsanaṃ yogyam uttamasya kathaṃ na me ।। 

kathaṃ me sukṛtaṃ tuccham uttamasyottamaṃ katham 
iti śrutvā vacas tasya sunītir nītimacchiśoḥ ।। 

kiṃcid ucchvasya śanakaiḥ śiśuśokopaśāntaye 
svabhāvamadhurāṃ vāṇīṃ vaktuṃ samupacakrame ।। 

ayi tāta mahābuddhe viśuddhenāntarātmanā 
nivedayāmi te sarvaṃ māvamāne matiṃ kṛthāḥ ।। 

tayā yad uktaṃ tat sarvaṃ tathyam eva na cānyathā 
yadi sā mahiṣī rājño rājñīnām ativallabhā ।। 

mahāsukṛtasaṃbhārair uttamaś cottamodare 
uvāsa tasyāḥ puṇyāyā nṛpasiṃhāsanocitaḥ ।। 

ātapatraṃ ca candrābhaṃ śubhe cāpi hi cāmare 
bhadrāsanaṃ tathoccaṃ ca sindhurāś ca madotkaṭāḥ ।। 

turaṃgamāś ca turagā anādhivyādhi jīvitam 
niḥsapatnaṃ śubhaṃ rājyaṃ prāpyaṃ viṣṇuprasādataḥ ।। 

ity ākarṇya sunītyās tan mātur vākyam aninditam 
saunīteyo dhruvo vācam ādade vaktum uttaram ।। 

janayitri sunīte me śṛṇu vākyam anākulam 
uttānacaraṇād anyan nāstīti me matiḥ śubhe ।। 

siddhārtho asmy amba yady asti kaścid āśritakāmadhuk 
adyaiva sakalārādhyaṃ tam ārādhya jagatpatim ।। 

tattadāsāditaṃ viddhi padam anyair durāsadam 
ekam eva hi sāhāyyaṃ mātar me kartum arhasi ।। 

anujñāṃ dehi me viṣṇuṃ yathā cārādhayāmy aham ।। b

anujñātuṃ na śaknomi tvām uttānaśayāṅgaja ।। d

saptāṣṭavarṣadeśīyaḥ krīḍāyogyo asi putraka 
tvadekatanayā tāta tvadādhāraikajīvitā ।। 

labdho asi katibhiḥ kaṣṭhair iṣṭā saṃprārthya devatāḥ 
yadā yadā bahir yāsi raṃtuṃ tricaturaṃ padam 
tadā tadā mama prāṇas tāta tvām upagacchati ।। 

adya yāvat pitā mātā tvaṃ cottānapado vibhuḥ 
adyaprabhṛti me mātā pitā viṣṇur na śaṃśayaḥ ।। 

viṣṇor ārādhane nāhaṃ vāraye tvāṃ suputraka 
jihvā me śatadhā yāti yadi tvāṃ vārayāmi bhoḥ ।। 

ity anujñām iva prāpya jananīcaraṇāmbujau 
parikramya praṇamyātha tapase sa dhruvo yayau ।। 

tayāpi dhairyasūtreṇa sunītyā parigumphya ca 
tatrendīvarajā mālā dhruvasyopāyanīkṛtā ।। 

mātrā tanmārgarakṣārthaṃ tadā tadanugīkṛtāḥ 
parair avāryaprasarāḥ svāśīrvādāḥ paraḥśatāḥ ।। 

sarvatrāvatu te putra śaṅkhacakagadādharaḥ 
nārāyaṇo jagadvyāpī prabhuḥ kāruṇyavāridhiḥ ।। 

svasaudhāt sa vinirgatya bālo bālaparākramaḥ 
anukūlena marutā darśitādhvāviśad vanam ।। 

sa mātṛdaivatobhijñaḥ kevalaṃ rājavartmani 
na veda kānanādhvānaṃ kṣaṇaṃ dadhyau nṛpātmajaḥ ।। 

puropavanam āsādya cintayāmasa so arbhakaḥ 
kiṃ karomi kva gacchāmi ko me sāhāyyado bhavet ।। 

evam unmīlya nayane yāvat paśyati sa dhruvaḥ 
tāvad dadarśa saptarṣīn atarkitagatīn vane ।। 

atha dṛṣṭvā sa saptarṣīn saptasaptatitejasaḥ 
bhāgyasūtrair ivākṛṣyo-panītān pramumoda ha ।। 

tilakāṅkitasadbhālān kuśopagrahitāṅgulīn 
kṛṣṇājinopaviṣṭāṃś ca brahmasūtrair alaṃkṛtān ।। 

upagamya vinamrāṃsaḥ prabaddhakarasaṃpuṭaḥ 
dhruvo vijñāpayaṃcakre praṇamya lalitaṃ vacaḥ ।। 

avaita māṃ munivarāḥ sunītyudarasaṃbhavam 
uttānapādatanayaṃ dhruvaṃ nirviṇṇamānasam ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvorjasvalaṃ bālaṃ svabhāvamadhurākṛtim 
anarghyanayane pathyaṃ mṛdugambhīrabhāṣiṇam ।। 

upopaveśya śiśukaṃ procus te vismitā bhṛśam 
tavādyāpi na jānīmo vatsa nirvedakāraṇam ।। 

anavāptābhilāṣāṇāṃ vairāgyaṃ jāyate nṛṇām 
saptadvīpapate rājñaḥ kumāras tvaṃ tathā katham ।। 

kim asmābhir aho kāryaṃ kas tavāsti manorathaḥ ।। b

munayo mama yo bandhur uttamaś cottamottamaḥ ।। d

pitrā pradattaṃ tasyāstu tad bhadrāsanam uttamam 
bhavatkṛtaṃ hi sāhāyyaṃ etad icchāmi suvratāḥ ।। 

ananyanṛpabhuktaṃ yad yad anyebhyaḥ samucchritam 
indrādiduravāpaṃ yat kathaṃ labhyeta tat padam ।। 

iti śrutvā vacas tasya munayo bālakasya tu 
yathārtham eva pratyūcur marīcyādyās tadā dhruvam ।। 

anāsvāditagovindapadāmbujarajorasaḥ 
manorathapathātītaṃ sphītaṃ nākalayet phalam ।। 

anarcitācyutapadaḥ padam āsādayet katham 
indrādiduravāpaṃ yan mānavaiḥ sudurāsadam ।। 

na hi dūre padaṃ tasya sarvāsāṃ saṃpadām iha 
kamalākāntakāntāṅghrikamalaṃ yaḥ suśīlayet ।। 

yasya smaraṇamātreṇa mahāpātakasaṃtatiḥ 
paramāntakam āpnoti sa viṣṇuḥ sarvado dhruva ।। 

yad āhuḥ paramaṃ brahma pradhānapuruṣāt param 
yanmāyayā kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ sa viṣṇu kīrtito arthadaḥ ।। 

yo yajñapuruṣo viṣṇur vedavedyo janārdanaḥ 
antarātmāsya jagataḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ kiṃ na yacchati ।। 

yad bhūnartanavartinyaḥ siddhayo aṣṭau nṛpātmaja 
tam ārādhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ caturvargo na dūrataḥ ।। 

satyam uktaṃ dvijendrā vo viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ prati 
kathaṃ sa bhagavān ijyaḥ sa vidhiś copadiśyatām ।। 

prabhūtado bhaved yo vai durārādhyatamo bhavet 
bālo ahaṃ rājaputro ahaṃ duḥkhaṃ naiva mayā kṣamam ।। 

tiṣṭhatā gacchatā vāpi svapatā jāgratā tathā 
śayānenopaviṣṭena vedyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā ।। 

putrān kalatraṃ mitrāṇi rājyaṃ svargāpavargakam 
vāsudevaṃ japan martyaḥ sarvaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।। 

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa vāsudevātmakena ca 
dhyāyaṃś caturbhujaṃ viṣṇuṃ japtvā siddhiṃ na ko gataḥ ।। 

pitāmahena cāpy eṣa mahāmantra upāsitaḥ 
manunā rājyakāmena vaiṣṇavena nṛpātmaja ।। 

tvam apy etena mantreṇa vāsudevaparo bhava 
yathābhilaṣitām ṛddhiṃ kṣipraṃ prāpsyasi sattama ।। 

ity uktvāntarhitāḥ sarve mahātmāno munīśvarāḥ 
vāsudevamanā bhūtvā dhruvo api tapase yayau ।। 

dhruvaḥ sarvārthadaṃ mantraṃ japan madhuvane tapaḥ 
sa cakre yamunātīre munidiṣṭena vartmanā ।। 

śraddhānvitena japatā ca tapaḥprabhāvāt sākṣād ivābjanayanaṃ dadṛśe hṛdīśam 
divyākṛtiṃ sapadi tena tataḥ sa eva harṣāt punaḥ sa prajajāpa nṛpātmabhūtaḥ ।। 

kṣuttarṣavarṣaghanavātamahoṣṇatādi śārīraduḥkhakulam asya na kiṃcanābhūt 
magne manasy anupameyasukhāmburāśau rājñaḥ śiśur na ca viveda śarīravārtām ।। 

vighnāś ca tasya kila śaṅkitadevasṛṣṭā bālasya tīvratapaso viphalā babhūvuḥ 
śītātapādir iva viṣṇumayaṃ muniṃ hi prādeśikā na khalu dharṣayituṃ kṣamante ।। 

atha bhaktajanapriyaḥ prabhuḥ śiśunā dhyānabalena toṣitaḥ 
varadaḥ patagendravāhano harir āgāt svajanaṃ tam īkṣitum ।। 

maṇipiṇḍakamaulirājito vilasadratnamahāghanacchaviḥ 
sa babhāv udayādrimatsarād dhṛtabālārka ivāsitācalaḥ ।। 

sa rājasūnuṃ tapasi sthitaṃ taṃ dhruvaṃ dhruvasnigdhadṛg ity uvāca 
dantāṃśusaṃjñair amitapravāhaiḥ prakṣālayan reṇum ivāsya gātre ।। 

varaṃ varaṃ vatsa vṛṇīṣva yas te manogatas tvattapasāsmi tuṣṭaḥ 
dhyānena te cendriyanigraheṇa manonirodhena ca duṣkareṇa ।। 

śṛṇvan vacas tat sakalaṃ gambhīram unmīlitākṣaḥ sahasā dadarśa 
sve cintyamānaṃ tv idam eva mūrtaṃ puraḥsthitaṃ brahma caturbhujaṃ saḥ ।। 

dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇaṃ rājasutaḥ supūjyaṃ puras trayīśaṃ kim iha bravīmi 
kiṃ vā karomīti sasaṃbhramaḥ sa tu na cābravīt kiṃcana no cakāra ।। 

harṣāśrupūrṇaḥ pulakāñcitāṅgas trilokanātheti vadann athoccaiḥ 
daṇḍapraṇāmāya papāta bhūmau pravepamānabhru hareḥ puraḥ sa hi ।। 

daṇḍavat praṇipatyātha paritaḥ pariluṇṭhya ca 
roroda harṣeṇa ciraṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ jagato gurum ।। 

nāradena sanandena sanakena ca saṃśrutam 
anyaiḥ sanatkumārādyair yogibhir yogināṃ varam ।। 

kāruṇyabāṣpanīrārdraṃ puṇḍarīkavilocanam 
dhruvam utthāpayāṃcakre cakrī dhṛtvā kareṇa tam ।। 

haris tu paripasparśa tadaṅgaṃ dhūlidhūsaram 
karābhyāṃ komalābhyāṃ sa pariṣvajyāha taṃ hariḥ ।। 

varaṃ varaya bho bāla yat te manasi vartate 
tad dadāmi na saṃdeho nādeyaṃ vidyate tava ।। 

tato varaṃ rājaśiśur yayāce viṣṇuṃ varaṃ te stavaśaktim eva 
taṃ mūrtivijñānanibhena devaḥ pasparśa śaṅkhena mukhe amalena ।। 

atha suramunidattajñānacandreṇa samyag vimalitam iva cittaṃ pūrṇam eva dhruvasya 
tribhuvanaguruśaṅkhasparśajajñānabhānān udayati nitarāntaḥ sādhu tuṣṭāva hṛṣṭaḥ ।। 
akhilamunijananivahanamitacaraṇaḥ । capalacaritaḥ । devārādhitapādajalaḥ । sajalajaladharaśyāmaḥ । śamitasaubhapatiśālvādhāmā । abhirāmarāmātivinayakṛtanavarasarasāpahatendriyasuraramaṇīvihitāntaḥkaraṇānandaḥ । adhananijadvijamitroddharaṇadhīraḥ । avadhīritasuranāthanāthitavipakṣapakṣaḥ । ṛkṣarājabilapraveśāpahatasyamantakāpamārjita nijāpavādadūritahṛtatrailokyabhāraḥ । dvārakāvāsanirataḥ । svaritamadhuraveṇuvādanaśravaṇāmṛtaprakaṭita atīndriyajñānaḥ । dvijadhenubhṛṅgagaṇais tyaktanijanijāhāraḥ । saṃsāradustarapārāvārasamuttāraṇāṅghripotaḥ । svapratāpānalahutakālayavanaḥ । vanamālādharavaramaṇikuṇḍalālaṃkṛtaśravaṇaḥ । nānāprasiddhābhidhānaḥ । nigamavibudhamunijanavacanamanogocaraḥ । kanakapiśaṅgakauśeyavāso bhagavān bhṛgupadakaustubhavibhūṣitoraḥsthalaḥ । svadayitākrūranijajananīgokulapālakacatur bhujaśaṅkhacakragadāpadmatulasīnavadala dāmahārakeyūrakaṭakamukuṭālaṃkṛtaḥ । sunandanādibhāgavatopāsitaviśvarūpaḥ । purāṇapuruṣottamaḥ । uttamaślokaḥ । lokāvāso vāsudevaḥ । śrīdevakījaṭharasaṃbhūtaḥ । bhūtapativirañcinatacaraṇāravindaḥ । vṛndāvanakṛtakeligopikājanaśramāpahaḥ । satataṃ saṃpāditasujanakāmaḥ । kundanibhaśaṅkhadharam indunibhavaktraṃ sundarasudarśanam udāratarahāsaṃ vidvajjanavanditam idaṃ ye rūpam atihṛdyam akhileśvaraṃ nato asmi । 
sthānābhikāmī tapasi sthito aham tvāṃ dṛṣṭavān sādhumunīndraguhyam 
kācaṃ vicinvann iva divyaratnaṃ svāmin kṛtārtho asmi varān na yāci ।। 

apūrvadṛṣṭe tava pādapadme dṛṣṭvā dṛḍhaṃ nātha na hi tyajāmi 
kāmān na yāce sa hi ko api mūḍho yaḥ kalpavṛkṣāt tuṣamātram icchet ।। 

tvāṃ mokṣabījaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannaḥ śaknomi bhoktuṃ na bahiḥsukhāni 
ratnākare deva sati svanāthe vibhūṣaṇaṃ kācamayaṃ na yuktam ।। 

ato na yāce varam īśa yuṣmat pādābjabhaktiṃ satataṃ mamāstu 
imaṃ varaṃ devavara prayaccha punaḥ punas tvām idam eva yāce ।। 

ity ātmasaṃdarśanalabdhadivyajñānaṃ gadantaṃ bhagavāñ jagāda ।। 

ārādhya viṣṇuṃ kim anena labdhaṃ mā bhūñjane apīttham asādhuvādaḥ 
sthānaṃ paraṃ prāpnuhi yan mataṃ te kālena māṃ prāpsyasi śuddhabhāvaḥ ।। 

ādhārabhūtaḥ sakalagrahāṇāṃ kalpadrumaḥ sarvajanaiś ca vandyaḥ 
mama prasādāt tava sā ca mātā mamāntike yā ca sunītir āryā ।। 

taṃ sādhayitveti varair mukundaḥ svam ālayaṃ dṛśyavapur jagāma 
tyaktvā śanair divyavapuḥ svabhaktaṃ muhuḥ parāvṛttya samīkṣamāṇaḥ ।। 

tāvac ca sadyaḥ surasiddhasaṅghaḥ śrīviṣṇutadbhaktasamāgamaṃ tam 
dṛṣṭvātha varṣan surapuṣpavṛṣṭiṃ tuṣṭāva harṣād dhruvam avyayaṃ ca ।। 

śriyābhimatyā ca sunītisūnur vibhāti devair api vandyamānaḥ 
yo ayaṃ nṛṇāṃ kīrtanadarśanābhyām āyur yaśo vardhayati śriyaṃ ca ।। 

itthaṃ dhruvaḥ prāpa padaṃ durāpaṃ hareḥ prasādān na ca citram etat 
tasmin prasanne dvijarājapatre na durlabhaṃ bhaktajaneṣu kiṃcit ।। 

sūryamaṇḍalamānāt tu dviguṇaṃ somamaṇḍalam 
pūrṇe śatasahasre dve tasmān nakṣatramaṇḍalam ।। 

dve lakṣe api budhasyāpi sthānaṃ nakṣatramaṇḍalāt 
tāvatpramāṇabhāge tu budhasyāpy uśanā sthitaḥ ।। 

aṅgārako api śukrasya tāvanmāne vyavasthitaḥ 
lakṣadvayaṃ tu bhaumasya sthito devapurohitaḥ ।। 

saurir bṛhaspateś cordhvaṃ dvilakṣe tu vyavasthitaḥ 
tasmāc chanaiścarād ūrdhvaṃ lakṣe saptarṣimaṇḍalam ।। 

saptarṣimaṇḍalād ūrdhvam ekaṃ lakṣaṃ dhruvaḥ sthitaḥ 
meḍhībhūtaḥ samastasya jyotiścakrasya sattama ।। 

svabhāvāt tapati viprendra adhaś cordhvaṃ ca raśmibhiḥ 
kālasaṃkhyāṃ trilokasya sa karoti yuge yuge ।। 

janas tapas tathā satyam etāṃl lokān dvijottama 
brahmaṇā muniśārdūla viṣṇubhaktivivardhitaḥ ।। 

ūrdhvagatair dvijaśreṣṭha raśmibhis tapate raviḥ 
adhogataiś ca bhūrlokaṃ dyotate dīrghadīdhitiḥ ।। 

sarvapāpaharaḥ sūryaḥ kartā tribhuvanasya ca 
chatravat pratipaśyeta maṇḍalān maṇḍalaṃ param ।। 

ādityamaṇḍalādhastād bhuvarlokaṃ pratiṣṭhitam 
trailokyasyeśvaratvaṃ ca viṣṇudattaṃ śatakratoḥ ।। 

lokapālaiḥ sa sahito lokān rakṣati dharmataḥ 
vaset svarge mahābhāga devendraḥ sa tu kīrtimān ।। 

tato adhastān mune cedaṃ pātālaṃ viddhi saprabham 
na tatra tapate sūryo na rātrir na niśākaraḥ ।। 

divyasvarūpam āsthāya tapanti satataṃ janāḥ 
pātālasthā dvijaśreṣṭha dīpyamanāḥ svatejasā ।। 

svarlokāt tu maharlokaḥ koṭimātre vyavasthitaḥ 
tato yojanamātreṇa dviguṇo maṇḍalena tu ।। 

janalokaḥ sthito vipra pañcamo munisevitaḥ 
tatropari tapolokaś caturbhiḥ koṭibhiḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

satyaloko aṣṭakoṭībhis tapolokoparisthitaḥ 
sarve chatrākṛtijñeyā bhuvanoparisaṃsthitāḥ ।। 

brahmalokād viṣṇuloko dviguṇaś ca vyavasthitaḥ 
vārāhe tasya māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ lokacintakaiḥ ।। 

tataḥ paraṃ dvijaśreṣṭha sthitaḥ paramapuruṣaḥ 
brahmāṇḍāt paramaḥ sākṣān nirlepaḥ puruṣaḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

paśupāśair vimucyeta tapojñānasamanvitaḥ 
iti te saṃsthitiḥ proktā bhūgolasya mayānagha 
yas tu samyag imāṃ vetti sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

lokasya saṃsthānakaro aprameyo viṣṇur nṛsiṃho naradevapūjitaḥ 
yuge yuge viṣṇur anādimūrtimān āsthāya viśvaṃ paripāti duṣṭahā ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ekatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

sahasrānīkasya harer avatārāṃś ca śārṅgiṇaḥ 
sāṃprataṃ śrotum icchāmi tan me vada mahāmate ।। 

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi caritaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ 
sahasrānīkasya harer avatārāṃś ca me śṛṇu ।। 

sahasrānīko abhiṣikto nijarājye dvijottamaiḥ 
pālayāmasa dharmeṇa rājyaṃ sa tu nṛpātmajaḥ ।। 

tasya pālayato rājyaṃ rājaputrasya dhīmataḥ 
bhaktir babhūva deveśe narasiṃhe surottame ।। 

taṃ draṣṭum āgataḥ sākṣād viṣṇubhaktaṃ bhṛguḥ purā 
arghyapādyāsanai rājā tam abhyarcyābravīd idam ।। 

pāvito ahaṃ muniśreṣṭha sāṃprataṃ tava darśanāt 
tvaddarśanam apuṇyānāṃ kalāv asmin sudurlabham ।। 

narasiṃhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya devadevaṃ sanātanam 
ārādhayitum icchāmi vidhānaṃ tatra me vada ।। 

avatārān aśeṣāṃś ca devadevasya cakriṇaḥ 
śrotum icchāmi sakalāṃs tān puṇyān api me vada ।। 

śṛṇu bhūpālaputra tvaṃ na hi kaścit kalau yuge 
harau bhaktiṃ karoty atra nṛsiṃhe cātibhaktimān ।। 

svabhāvād yasya bhaktiḥ syān narasiṃhe surottame 
tasyārayaḥ praṇaśyanti kāryasiddhiś ca jāyate ।। 

tvam atīva harer bhaktaḥ pāṇḍuvaṃśe api sattamaḥ 
tena te nikhilaṃ vakṣye śṛṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ ।। 

yaḥ kuryāc chobhanaṃ veśma narasiṃhasya bhaktimān 
sa sarvapāpanirmukto viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt ।। 

pratimāṃ lakṣaṇopetāṃ narasiṃhasya kārayet 
sa sarvapāpanirmukto viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt ।। 

pratiṣṭhāṃ narasiṃhasya yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi 
niṣkāmo naraśārdūla dehabādhāt pramucyate ।। 

narasiṃhaṃ pratiṣṭhapya yaḥ pūjām ācaren naraḥ 
tasya kāmāḥ prasidhyanti paramaṃ padam āpnuyāt ।। 

brahmādayaḥ surāḥ sarve viṣṇum ārādhya te purā 
svaṃ svaṃ padam anuprāptāḥ keśavasya prasādataḥ ।। 

ye ye nṛpavarā rājan māndhātṛpramukhā nṛpāḥ 
te te viṣṇuṃ samārādhya svargalokam ito gatāḥ ।। 

yas tu pūjayate nityaṃ narasiṃhaṃ sureśvaram 
sa svargamokṣabhāgī syān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

tasmād ekamanā bhūtvā yāvajjīvaṃ pratijñayā 
arcanān narasiṃhasya prāpsyase svābhivāñchitam ।। 

vidhivat sthāpayed yas tu kārayitvā janārdanam 
na tu nirgamanaṃ tasya viṣṇulokād bhaven nṛpa ।। 

naro nṛsiṃhaṃ tam anantavikramaṃ surāsurair arcitapādapaṅkajam 
saṃsthāpya bhaktyā vidhivac ca pūjayet payāti sākṣāt parameśvaraṃ harim ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite dvātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

harer arcāvidhiṃ puṇyāṃ śrotum icchāmi sattvataḥ 
tvatprasādād viśeṣeṇa bhagavan prabravīhi me ।। 

saṃmārjanakaro yaś ca narasiṃhasya mandire 
yat puṇyaṃ labhate tadvad upalepanakṛṇ naraḥ ।। 

śuddhodakena yat puṇyaṃ snāpite keśave bhavet 
kṣīrasnānena yat puṇyaṃ dadhnā ca madhunā tathā 
ghṛtasnānena yat puṇyaṃ pañcagavyena yad bhavet ।। 

kṣālite coṣṇatoyena pratimāyāṃ ca bhaktitaḥ 
karpūrāgurutoyena miśreṇa snāpitena ca ।। 

arghyadānena yat puṇyaṃ pādyācamanadānake 
mantreṇa snāpite yac ca vastradānena yad bhavet ।। 

śrīkhaṇḍakuṅkumābhyāṃ tu arcite kiṃ phalaṃ bhavet 
puṣpair abhyarcite yac ca yat phalaṃ dhūpadīpayoḥ ।। 

naivedyair yat phalaṃ proktaṃ pradakṣiṇakṛte tu yat 
namaskārakṛte yac ca phalaṃ yas stotragītayoḥ ।। 

tālavṛntapradānena cāmarasya ca yad bhavet 
dhvajapradāne yad viṣṇoḥ śaṅkhadānena yad bhavet ।। 

etac cānyac ca yat kiṃcid ajñānān na pracoditam 
tat sarvaṃ kathaya brahman bhaktasya mama keśave ।। 

iti saṃprerito vipras tena rājñā bhṛgus tadā 
mārkaṇḍeyaṃ niyujyātha kathane sa gato muniḥ ।। 

so api tasmin mudāyukto haribhaktyā viśeṣataḥ 
rājñe pravaktum ārebhe bhṛguṇā codito muniḥ ।। 

rājaputra śṛṇuṣvedaṃ haripūjāvidhiṃ kramāt 
viṣṇubhaktasya vakṣyāmi tavāhaṃ pāṇḍuvaṃśaja ।। 

narasiṃhasya nityaṃ ca yaḥ saṃmārjanam ārabhet 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke sa modate ।। 

gomayena mṛdā toyair yaḥ karoty upalepanam 
sa cākṣayaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। 

atrārthe yat purāvṛttam itihāsaṃ purātanam 
yac chrutvā sarvapāpebhyo muktir bhavati sattama ।। 

purā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā pañcabhir bhrātṛbhir yutaḥ 
draupadyā saha rājendra kānanaṃ vicacāra ha ।। 

śūlakaṇṭakaniṣkrāntās tatas te pañca pāṇḍavāḥ 
nārado api gato nākaṃ juṣṭvedaṃ tīrtham uttamam ।। 

tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā prasthitas tīrtham uttamam 
darśanaṃ munimukhyasya tīrthadharmopadeśinaḥ ।। 

cintayati ca dharmātmā krodhapaiśunyavarjitaḥ 
dānavo bahuromā ca tathā sthūlaśirā nṛpa ।। 

pāṇḍavān gacchato vīkṣya dānavo draupadīcchayā 
kṛtvā bhūpa mune rupaṃ bahuromā gatas tadā ।। 

praṇidhānaṃ vidhāyātha āsīnaḥ kuśaviṣṭare 
bibhrat kamaṇḍaluṃ pārśve darbhasūcīṃ tathā kare ।। 

akṣamālāṃ japan mantraṃ svanāsāgraṃ nirīkṣayan 
sa dṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍavais tatra revāyāṃ vanacāribhiḥ ।। 

tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā taṃ praṇamya sahānujaḥ 
jagāda vacanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāgyenāsi mahāmune ।। 

tīrthāni rudradehāyāḥ sugopyāni nivedaya 
munīnāṃ darśanaṃ nātha śrutaṃ dharmopadeśakam ।। 

yāvan munim uvācedaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ 
tāvat sthūlaśirāḥ prāpto munirūpadharo aparaḥ ।। 

jalpann ity āturaṃ vākyaṃ ko nāmāsty atra rakṣakaḥ 
bhayāturaṃ naro jīvaṃ yo rakṣec charaṇāgatam ।। 

tasyānantaphalaṃ syād vai kiṃ punar māṃ dvijottamam 
ekato medinīdānaṃ merubhūdharadakṣiṇam ।। 

anyato hy ārtajīvānāṃ prāṇasaṃśayavāraṇam 
dvijaṃ dhenuṃ striyaṃ bālaṃ piḍyamānaṃ ca durjanaiḥ ।। 

upekṣeta naro yas tu sa ca gacchati rauravam 
atha māṃ hṛtasarvasvaṃ prāṇatyāgaparāyaṇam ।। 

ko rakṣati naro vīraḥ parābhūtaṃ hi dānavaiḥ 
gṛhītvā cākṣamālāṃ me tathā subhakamaṇḍalum ।। 

nihato ahaṃ karāghātais tathā khāṭo manoharaḥ 
gṛhītaṃ mama sarvasvaṃ dānavena durātmanā ।। 

ity ākarṇya vacaḥ klībaṃ pāṇḍavā jātasaṃbhramāḥ 
yānti romāñcitā bhūyo vidhāyāgniṃ ca taṃ munim ।। 

vimucya draupadīṃ tatra muneḥ pārśve mahātmanaḥ 
tato dūrataraṃ prāptāḥ saṃrambhāt te ca pāṇḍavāḥ ।। 

tato yudhiṣṭhiro avocat kiṃ ca no nātra dṛśyate 
kṛṣṇāsaṃrakṣaṇārthāya vraja vyāvartya cārjuna ।। 

tato arjuno viniṣkrānto bandhuvākyapraṇoditaḥ 
tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā satyāṃ vācam akalpayat ।। 

nirīkṣya maṇḍalaṃ bhānos tadā sugahane vane 
mama satyāc ca sukṛtād dharmasaṃbhāṣaṇāt prabho ।। 

tathyaṃ śaṃsantu tridaśā mama saṃśayabhājinaḥ 
tato ambare abhavad vāṇī tadā bhūpāśarīriṇī ।। 

dānavo ayaṃ mahārāja muniḥ sthūlaśirāḥ sthitaḥ 
nāsāv upadrutaḥ kena māyaiṣāsya durātmanaḥ ।। 

tato bhīmaḥ karāghātair naśyamānaṃ hi dānavam 
saṃrambhāt kupito atyarthaṃ maulideśe jaghāna tam ।। 

so api rūpaṃ nijaṃ prāpya raudraṃ bhīmam atāḍayat 
tatra yuddhaṃ pravavṛte dāruṇaṃ bhīmadaityayoḥ ।। 

kaṣṭād babhañja bhīmo api tasya sthūlaṃ śiro vane 
arjuno api samāyāto naiva paśyati taṃ munim ।। 

tathā ca draupadīṃ bhūyaḥ sādhvīṃ kāntāṃ ca vallabhām 
tato vṛkṣaṃ samāruhya yāvat paśyati cārjunaḥ ।। 

tāvad vidhāya tāṃ skandhe śīghraṃ dhāvati dānavaḥ 
saṃhṛtā yāti duṣṭena rudatī kurarī yathā ।। 

kurvatī bhīmabhīmeti dharmaputreti vādinī 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa yayau vīraḥ śabdair saṃnādayan diśaḥ ।। 

pādanyāsoruvegena prabhagnāḥ pādapā bhṛśam 
tato daityo api tāṃ tanvīṃ vihāyāśu palāyitaḥ ।। 

tathāpi cārjuno tasya kopān muñcati nāsuram 
patito medinīpṛṣṭhe tāvad eva caturbhujaḥ ।। 

pīte cavāsasī bibhrat śaṅkhacakrāyudhāni ca 
tataḥ sa vismayākrānto natvā pārtho vaco avadat ।। 

kathaṃ kṛtaiṣā bhagavaṃs tvayā māyātra vaiṣṇavī 
mayāpy apakṛtaṃ nātha tat kṣamasva namo astu te ।। 

nūnam ajñānabhāvena karmaitad dāruṇaṃ mayā 
tat kṣantavyaṃ jagannātha caitanyaṃ mānave kutaḥ ।। 

nāhaṃ kṛṣṇo mahābāho bahuromāsmi dānavaḥ 
upayāto harer dehaṃ pūrvakarmaprabhāvataḥ ।। 

bahuroman purvajātiṃ karma me śaṃsa tattvataḥ 
kena karmavipākena viṣṇoḥ sārūpyam āptavān ।। 

śṛṇv arjuna mahābhāga sahito bhrātṛbhir mama 
caritaṃ citram atyarthaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ mudavardhanam ।। 

aham āsaṃ purā rājā somavaṃśasamudbhavaḥ 
jayadhvaja iti khyāto nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।। 

viṣṇor devālaye nityaṃ saṃmārjanaparāyaṇaḥ 
upaleparataś caiva dīpadāne samudyataḥ ।। 

vītihotra iti khyāta āsīt sādhupurohitaḥ 
mama taccaritaṃ dṛṣṭvā vipro vismayam āgataḥ ।। 

kadācid upaviṣṭaṃ taṃ rājānaṃ viṣṇutatparam 
apṛcchad vītihotras taṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।। 

rājan paramadharmajña haribhaktaparāyaṇa 
viṣṇubhaktimatāṃ puṃsāṃ śreṣṭho asi puruṣarṣabha ।। 

saṃmārjanaparo nityaṃ upaleparatas tathā 
tan me vada mahābhāga tvayā kiṃ viditaṃ phalam ।। 

karmāṇy anyāni santy eva viṣṇoḥ priyatarāṇi vai 
tathāpi tvaṃ mahābhāga etayoḥ satatodyataḥ ।। 

sarvātmanā mahāpuṇyaṃ janeśa viditaṃ tava 
tad brūhi yady aguhyaṃ ca prītir mayi tavāsti cet ।। 

śṛṇuṣva vipraśārdūla mamaiva caritaṃ purā ।। 

jātismaratvāj jānāmi śrotṝṇāṃ vismayāvaham 
pūrvajanmani viprendra raivato nāma vāḍavaḥ ।। 

ayājyayājako ahaṃ vai sadaiva grāmayājakaḥ 
piśuno niṣṭhuraś caiva apaṇyanāṃ ca vikrayī ।। 

niṣiddhakarmācaraṇāt parityaktaḥ svabandhubhiḥ 
mahāpāparato nityaṃ brahmadveṣaratas tathā ।। 

paradāraparadravyalolupo jantuhiṃsakaḥ 
madyapānarato nityaṃ brahmadveṣaratas tathā ।। 

evaṃ paparato nityaṃ bahuśo mārgarodhakṛt 
kadācit kāmacāro ahaṃ gṛhītvā brāhmaṇastriyaḥ ।। 

śūnyaṃ pūjādibhir viṣṇor mandiraṃ prāptavān niśi 
svavastraprāntato brahman kiyadaṃśaḥ sa mārjitaḥ ।। 

pradīpaḥ sthāpitas tatra suratārthād dvijottama 
tenāpi mama duṣkarma niḥśeṣaṃ kṣayam āgatam ।। 

evaṃ sthitaṃ viṣṇugṛhe mayā bhogecchayā dvija 
tadaiva dīpakaṃ dṛṣṭvā āgatāḥ purapālakāḥ ।। 

cauryārthaṃ paradūto ayam ity uktvā mām apātayan 
khaḍgena tīkṣṇadhāreṇa śiraś chittvā ca te gatāḥ ।। 

divyaṃ vimānam āruhya prabhudāsasamanvitam 
gandharvair gīyamāno ahaṃ svargalokaṃ tadā gataḥ ।। 

tatra sthitvā brahmakalpaṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ dvijottamāḥ 
divyabhogasamāyukto divyarūpasamanvitaḥ ।। 

jāto ahaṃ puṇyayogād dhi somavaṃśasamudbhavaḥ 
jayadhvaja iti khyāto rājā rājīvalocanaḥ ।। 

tatrāpi kālavaśato mṛtaḥ svargam avāptavān 
indralokam anuprāpya rudralokaṃ tato gataḥ ।। 

rudralokād brahmalokaṃ gacchatā nārado muniḥ 
dṛṣṭaś ca namito naiva garvān me hasitaś ca saḥ ।। 

kupitaḥ śaptavān māṃ sa rākṣaso bhava bhūpate 
iti śāpaṃ samākarṇya dattaṃ tena dvijanmanā ।। 

prasādito mayā bhūpa prasādaṃ kṛtavān muniḥ 
yadā revāmaṭhe rājan dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥ ।। 

bhāryāpahāraṃ nayataḥ śāpamokṣo bhaviṣyati 
so aham arjuna bhūpāla dharmaputra yudhiṣṭhira ।। 

viṣṇoḥ sārūpyam agamaṃ yāmi vaikuṇṭham adya vai ।। b

ity uktvā garuḍārūḍho dharmaputrasya paśyataḥ ।। d

gatavān viṣṇubhavanaṃ yatra viṣṇuḥ śriyā saha 
saṃmārjanopalepābhyāṃ mahimā tena varṇitaḥ ।। 

avaśenāpi yat karma kṛtvemāṃ śriyam āgataḥ 
bhaktimadbhiḥ praśāntaiś ca kiṃ punaḥ samyagarcanāt ।। 

mārkaṇḍeyavacaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍuvaṃśasamudbhavaḥ 
sahasrānīkabhūpālo haripūjārato abhavat ।। 

tasmāc chṛṇuta viprendrā devo nārāyaṇo avyayaḥ 
jñānato ajñānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ ।। 

arcayadhvaṃ jagannāthaṃ bhūyo bhūyo vadāmy aham 
tartuṃ yadīcchatha dvijā dustaraṃ bhavasāgaram ।। 

ye arcayanti hariṃ bhaktāḥ praṇatārtiharaṃ harim 
te vandyās te prapūjyāś ca namasyāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasimhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite mārkaṇḍeyenopadiṣṭasaṃmārjanopalepaphalaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

punar eva dvijaśreṣṭha mārkaṇḍeya mahāmate 
nirmālyāpanayād viṣṇor yat puṇyaṃ tad vadasva me ।। 

nirmālyam apanīyātha toyena snāpya keśavam 
narasiṃhākṛtiṃ rājan sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 

sarvatīrthaphalaṃ prāpya yānārūḍho divaṃ vrajet 
śrīviṣṇoḥ sadanaṃ prāpya modate kālam akṣayam ।। 

āgaccha narasiṃheti āvāhyākṣatapuṣpakaiḥ 
etāvatāpi rājendra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 

dattvāsanam athārghyaṃ ca pādyam ācamanīyakam 
devadevasya vidhinā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 

snāpya toyena payasā narasiṃhaṃ narādhipa 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। 

snāpya dadhnā sakṛd yas tu nirmalaḥ priyadarśanaḥ 
viṣṇulokam avāpnoti pūjyamānaḥ surottamaiḥ ।। 

yaḥ karoti harer arcāṃ madhunā snāpayan naraḥ 
agniloke sa moditvā punar viṣṇupure vaset ।। 

ghṛtena snapanaṃ yas tu snānakāle viśeṣataḥ 
narasiṃhākṛteḥ kuryāc chaṅkhabherīnināditam ।। 

pāpakañcukam unmucya yathā jīrṇam ahis tvacam 
divyaṃ vimānam āsthāya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। 

pañcagavyena deveśaṃ yaḥ snāpayati bhaktitaḥ 
mantrapūrvaṃ mahārāja tasya puṇyam anantakam ।। 

yaś ca godhūmakaiś cūrṇair udvartyoṣṇena vāriṇā 
prakṣālya devadeveśaṃ vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt ।। 

pādapīṭhaṃ tu yo bhaktyā bilvapatrar nirgharṣitam 
uṣṇāmbunā ca prakṣālya sarvapāpair pramucyate ।। 

kuśapuṣpodakaiḥ snātvā brahmalokam avāpnuyāt 
ratnodakena sāvitraṃ kauberaṃ hemavāriṇā 
narasiṃhaṃ tu saṃsnāpya karpūrāguruvāriṇā ।। 

indraloke sa moditvā paścād viṣṇupure vaset 
puṇyodakena govindaṃ snāpya bhaktyā narottama ।। 

sāvitraṃ lokam āsādya viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
vastrābhyām arcanaṃ bhaktyā paridhāpya hariṃ hareḥ ।। 

somaloke ramitvā ca viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
kuṅkumāguruśrīkhaṇḍakardamair acyutākṛtim ।। 

ālipya bhaktyā rājendra kalpakoṭiṃ vased divi 
mallikāmālatījātiketakyaśokacampakaiḥ ।। 

puṃnāganāgabakulaiḥ padmair utpalajātibhiḥ 
tulasīkaravīraiś ca pālāśaiḥ sānukumbakaiḥ ।। 

etair anyaiś ca kusumaiḥ praśastair acyutaṃ naraḥ 
arcayed daśasuvarṇasya pratyekaṃ phalam āpnuyāt ।। 

mālāṃ kṛtvā yathālābham eteṣāṃ viṣṇum arcayet 
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca ।। 

divyāṃ vimānam āsthāya viṣṇuloke sa modate 
narasiṃhaṃ tu yo bhaktyā bilvapatrair akhaṇḍitaiḥ ।। 

niśchidraiḥ pūjayed yas tu tulasībhiḥ samanvitam 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

kāñcanena vimānena viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
māhiṣākhyaṃ guggulaṃ ca ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram ।। 

dhūpaṃ dadāti rājendra narasiṃhasya bhaktimān 
dhūpitaiḥ sarvadigbhyas tu sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ ।। 

apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇavimānena virājate 
vāyuloke sa moditvā paścād viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। 

ghṛtena vātha tailena dīpaṃ prajvālayen naraḥ 
viṣṇave vidhivad bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।। 

vihāya pāpakalilaṃ saharādityasaprabhaḥ 
jyotiṣmatā vimānena viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 

haviḥ śālyodanaṃ divān ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram 
nivedya narasiṃhāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā ।। 

samās tandulasaṃkhyāyā yāvatīs tāvatīr nṛpa 
viṣṇuloke mahābhogān bhuñjann āste sa vaiṣṇavaḥ ।। 

balinā vaiṣṇavenātha tṛptāḥ santo divaukasaḥ 
śāntiṃ tasya prayacchanti śriyam ārogyam eva ca ।। 

pradakṣiṇena caikena devadevasya bhaktitaḥ 
kṛtena yat phalaṃ nṝṇāṃ tac chṛṇuṣva nṛpātmaja ।। 

pṛthvīpradakṣiṇaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇupure vaset 
namaskāraḥ kṛto yena bhaktyā vai mādhavasya ca ।। 

dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyaṃ phalaṃ tenāptam añjasā 
stotrair japaiś ca devāgre yaḥ stauti madhusūdanam ।। 

sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
gītavādyādikaṃ nāṭyaṃ śaṅkhatūryādiniḥsvanaiḥ ।। 

yaḥ kārayati vai viṣṇoḥ sa yāti mandiraṃ naraḥ 
parvakāle viśeṣeṇa kāmagaḥ kāmarūpavān ।। 

susaṃgītavidaiś caiva sevyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ 
mahārhamaṇicitreṇa vimānena virājatā ।। 

svargāt svargam anuprāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
dhvajaṃ tu viṣṇave yas tu garuḍena samanvitam ।। 

dadyāt so api dhvajākīrṇavimānena virājatā 
viṣṇulokam avāpnoti sevyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। 

suvarṇābharaṇair divyair hārakeyūrakuṇḍalaiḥ 
mukuṭābharaṇādyaiś ca yo viṣṇuṃ pūjayen nṛpa ।। 

sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
indraloke vased dhīmān yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।। 

yo gāṃ payasvinīṃ viṣṇoḥ kapilāṃ saṃprayacchati 
ārādhya tam athāgre tu yat kiṃcid dagdham uttamam ।। 

tad dattvā narasiṃhāya viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
pitaras tasya modante śvetadvīpe ciraṃ nṛpa ।। 

evaṃ yaḥ pūjayed rājan narasiṃhaṃ narottamaḥ 
tasya svargāpavargau tu bhavato nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

yatraivaṃ pūjyate viṣṇur narasiṃho narair nṛpa 
na tatra vyādhidurbhikṣarājacaurādikaṃ bhayam ।। 

narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya vidhinānena mādhavam 
nānāsvargasukhaṃ bhuktvā na bhūyaḥ stanapo bhavet ।। 

nityaṃ sarpis tilair homo grāme yasmin pravartate 
na bhavet tasya grāmasya bhayaṃ vā tatra kutracit ।। 

anāvṛṣṭir māhāmārī doṣā no dāhakā nṛpa 
narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।। 

kārayel lakṣahomaṃ tu grāme yatra purādhipaḥ 
kṛte tasmin mayokte tu āgacchati na tadbhayam ।। 

dṛṣṭopasargamaraṇaṃ prajānām ātmanaś ca hi 
samyagārādhanīyaṃ tu narasiṃhasya mandire ।। 

śaṃkarāyatane cāpi koṭihomaṃ narādhipa 
kārayet saṃyatair vipraiḥ sabhojanasadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। 

kṛte tasmin nṛpaśreṣṭha narasiṃhaprasādataḥ 
upasargādimaraṇaṃ prajānām upaśāmyati ।। 

duḥsvapnadarśane ghore grahapīḍāsu cātmanaḥ 
homaṃ ca bhojanaṃ caiva tasya doṣaḥ praṇaśyati ।। 

ayane viṣuve caiva candrasūryagrahe tathā 
narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya lakṣahomaṃ tu kārayet ।। 

śāntir bhavati rājendra tasya tatsthānavāsinām 
evamādiphalopetaṃ narasiṃhārcanaṃ nṛpa ।। 

kuru tvaṃ bhūpateḥ putra yadi vāñchasi sadgatim 
ataḥ parataraṃ nāsti svargamokṣaphalapradam ।। 

narendraiḥ sukaraṃ kartuṃ devadevasya pūjanam 
santy araṇye hy amūlyāni patrapuṣpāṇi śākhinām ।। 

toyaṃ nadītaḍāgeṣu devaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ sthitaḥ 
mano niyamayed ekaṃ vidyāsādhanakarmaṇi ।। 

mano niyamitaṃ yena muktis tasya kare sthitā ।। 

ity evam uktaṃ bhṛgucoditena mayā tavehārcanam acyutasya 
dine dine tvaṃ kuru viṣṇupūjāṃ vadasva cānyat kathayāmi kiṃ te ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite śrīviṣṇoḥ pūjāvidhir nāma catustriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

aho mahat tvayā proktaṃ viṣṇvārādhanajaṃ phalam 
suptās te muniśārdūla ye viṣṇuṃ nārcayanti vai ।। 

tvatprasādāc chrutaṃ hy etan narasiṃhārcanakramam 
bhaktyā taṃ pūjayiṣyāmi koṭihomaphalaṃ vada ।। 

imam arthaṃ purā pṛṣṭaḥ śaunako guruṇā nṛpa 
yat tasmai kathayāmasa śaunakas tad vādami te ।। 

śaunakaṃ tu sukhāsīnaṃ paryapṛcchad bṛhaspatiḥ ।। b

lakṣahomasya yā bhūmiḥ koṭihomasya yā śubhā ।। d

tāṃ me kathaya viprendra homasya carite vidhim ।। b

ityukto guruṇā so atha lakṣahomādikaṃ vidhim ।। d

śaunako vaktum ārebhe yathāvan nṛpasattama ।। b

pravakṣyāmi yathāvat te śṛṇu devapurohita ।। d

lakṣahomamahābhūmiṃ tadviśuddhiṃ viśeṣataḥ 
yajñakarmaṇi śastāyā bhūmer lakṣaṇam uttamam ।। 

susaṃskṛtāṃ samāṃ snigdhāṃ pūrvapūrvam athottamām 
ūrumātraṃ khanitvā ca śodhayet tāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। 

bahiracchatayā tatra mṛdācchādya pralepayet 
pramāṇaṃ bāhumātraṃ tu sarvataḥ kuṇḍalakṣaṇam ।। 

caturasraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ tulyasūtreṇa kārayet 
upari mekhalāṃ kuryāc caturasrāṃ suvistarām ।। 

caturaṅgulamātraṃ tu ucchritāṃ sūtrasūtritām 
brāhmaṇān vedasaṃpannān brahmakarmasamanvitān ।। 

āmantrayed yathānyāyaṃ yajamāno viśeṣataḥ 
brahmacaryavrataṃ kuryus trirātraṃ te dvijātayaḥ ।। 

ahorātram upoṣyātha gāyatrīm ayutaṃ japet 
te śuklavāsasaḥ snātā gandhasrakpuṣpadhāriṇaḥ ।। 

śucayaś ca nirāhārāḥ saṃtuṣṭā saṃyatendriyāḥ 
kauśam āsanam āsīnā ekāgramanasaḥ punaḥ ।। 

ārabheyuś ca te yatnāt tato homam atandritāḥ 
bhūmim ālikhya cābhyukṣya yatnād agniṃ nidhāpayet ।। 

gṛhyoktena vidhānena homaṃ tatra ca homayet 
āghārāv ājyabhāgau ca juhuyāt pūrvam eva tu ।। 

yavadhānyatilair miśrāṃ gāyatryā prathamāhutim 
juhuyād ekacittena svāhākārānvitāṃ budhaḥ ।। 

gāyatrī chandasāṃ mātā brahmayoniḥ pratiṣṭhitā 
savitā devatā tasya viśvāmitras tathā ṛṣiḥ ।। 

tato vyāhṛtibhiḥ paścāj juhuyāc ca tilānvitam 
yāvat prapūryate saṃkhyā lakṣaṃ vā koṭir eva vā ।। 

tāvad dhomaṃ tilaiḥ kuryād acyutārcanapūrvakam 
dīnānāthajanebhyas tu yajamānaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। 

tāvac ca bhojanaṃ dadyād yāvad dhomaṃ samācaret 
samāpte dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād ṛtvigbhyaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ ।। 

yathārhatā na lobhena tataḥ śāntyudakena ca 
prokṣayed grāmamadhye tu vyādhitāṃs tu viśeṣataḥ ।। 

evaṃ kṛte tu homasya purasya nagarasya ca 
rāṣṭrasya ca mahābhāga rājño janapadasya ca 
sarvabādhāpraśamanī śāntir bhavati sarvadā ।। 

ity etac chaunakaproktaṃ kathitaṃ nṛpanandana 
lakṣahomādikavidhiṃ kāryaṃ rāṣṭre suśāntidam ।। 

grāme gṛhe vā purabāhyadeśe dvijair ayaṃ yatnakṛtaḥ purovidhiḥ 
tatrāpi śāntir bhavitā narāṇāṃ gavāṃ ca bhṛtyaiḥ saha bhūpateś ca ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe lakṣahomavidhir nāma pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

avatārān ahaṃ vakṣye devadevasya cakriṇaḥ 
tān śṛṇuṣva mahīpāla pavitrān pāpanāśanān ।। 

yathā matsyena rūpeṇa dattā vedāḥ svayaṃbhuve 
madhukaiṭabhau ca nidhanaṃ prāpitau ca mahātmanā ।। 

yathā kaurmeṇa rūpeṇa viṣṇunā mandaro dhṛtaḥ 
yathā pṛthvī dhṛtā rājan vārāheṇa mahātmanā ।। 

tenaiva nidhanaṃ prāpto yathā rājan mahābalaḥ 
hiraṇyākṣo mahāvīryo ditiputro mahātanuḥ ।। 

yathā hiraṇyakaśipus tridaśānām ariḥ purā 
narasiṃhena devena prāpito nidhanaṃ nṛpa ।। 

yathā baddho baliḥ pūrvaṃ vāmanena mahātmanā 
indras tribhuvanādhyakṣaḥ kṛtas tena nṛpātmaja ।। 

rāmeṇa bhūtvā ca yathā viṣṇunā rāvaṇo hataḥ 
sagaṇāś cādbhutā rājan rākṣasā devakaṇṭakāḥ ।। 

yathā paraśurāmeṇa kṣatram utsāditaṃ purā 
balabhadreṇa rāmeṇa yathā daityaḥ purā hataḥ ।। 

yathā kṛṣṇena kaṃsādyā hatā daityāḥ suradviṣaḥ 
kalau prāpte yathā buddho bhaven nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

kalkirūpaṃ samāsthāya yathā mlecchā nipātitāḥ 
samāpte tu kalau bhūyas tathā te kathayāmy aham ।। 

harer anantasya parākramaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti bhūpāla samāhitātmā 
mayocyamānaṃ ca vimucya pāpaṃ prayāti viṣṇoḥ padam atyudāram ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe hareḥ prādurbhāvānukramaṇe ṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

nānātvād avatārāṇām acyutasya mahātmanaḥ 
na śakyaṃ vistarād vaktuṃ tān bravīmi samāsataḥ ।। 

purā kila jagatsraṣṭā bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ 
anantabhogaśayane yoganidrāṃ samāgataḥ ।। 

atha tasya prasuptasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ 
śrotrābhyām apatat toye svedabindudvayaṃ nṛpa ।। 

madhukaiṭabhanāmānau tasmāj jātau mahābalau 
mahākāyau mahāvīryau mahābalaparākramau ।। 

acyutasya prasuptasya mahat padmam ajāyata 
nābhimadhye nṛpaśreṣṭha tasmin brahmābhyajāyata ।। 

sa cokto viṣṇunā rājan prajāḥ sṛja mahāmate 
tathety uktvā jagannāthaṃ brahmāpi kamalodbhavaḥ ।। 

vedaśāstravaśād yāvat prajā sraṣṭuṃ samudyataḥ 
tāvat tatra samāyātau tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau ।। 

āgatya vedaśāstrārthavijñānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ kṣaṇāt 
apakṛtya gatau ghorau dānavau baladarpitau ।। 

tataḥ padmodbhavo rājan jñānahīno abhavat kṣaṇāt 
duḥkhitaś cintayāmasa kathaṃ srakṣyāmi vai prajāḥ ।। 

coditas tvaṃ sṛjasveti prajā devena tat katham 
srakṣye ahaṃ jñānahīnas tu aho kaṣṭam upasthitam ।। 

iti saṃcintya duḥkhārto brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
yatnato vedaśāstrāṇi smarann api na dṛṣṭavān ।। 

tato viṣaṇṇacittas tu taṃ devaṃ puruṣottamam 
ekāgramanasā samyak śāstreṇa stotum ārabhat ।। 

oṃ namo vedanidhaye śāstrāṇāṃ nidhaye namaḥ 
vijñānanidhaye nityaṃ karmaṇāṃ nidhaye namaḥ ।। 

vidyādharāya devāya vāgīśāya namo namaḥ 
acintyāya namo nityaṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।। 

amūrtis tvaṃ mahābāho yajñamūrtir adhokṣaja 
sāmnāṃ mūrtis tvam evādya sarvadā sarvarūpavān ।। 

sarvajñānamayo asi tvaṃ hṛdi jñānamayo acyuta 
dehi me tvaṃ sarvajñānaṃ devadeva namo namaḥ ।। 

itthaṃ stutas tadā tena śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ 
brahmāṇam āha deveśo dāsye te jñānam uttamam ।। 

ity uktvā tu tadā viṣṇuś cintayāmasa pārthiva 
kenāsya nītaṃ vijñānaṃ kena rūpeṇa cādadhe ।। 

madhukaiṭabhakṛtaṃ sarvam iti jñātvā janārdanaḥ 
mātsyaṃ rūpaṃ samāsthāya bahuyojanam āyatam 
bahuyojanavistīrṇaṃ sarvajñānamayaṃ nṛpa ।। 

sa praviśya jalaṃ tūrṇaṃ kṣobhayāmasa taṃ hariḥ 
praviśya ca sa pātālaṃ dṛṣṭavān madhukaiṭabhau ।। 

tau mohayitvā tumulaṃ taj jñānaṃ jagṛhe hariḥ 
vedaśāstrāṇi munibhiḥ saṃstuto madhusūdanaḥ ।। 

ānīya brahmaṇe dattvā tyaktvā tan mātsyakaṃ nṛpa 
jagaddhitāya sa punar yoganidrāvaśaṃ gataḥ ।। 

tataḥ prabuddhau saṃkruddhau tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau 
āgatya dadṛśāte tu śayānaṃ devam avyayam ।। 

ayaṃ sa puruṣo dhūrta āvāṃ saṃmohya māyayā 
ānīya vedaśāstrāṇi dattvā śete atra sādhuvat ।। 

ity uktvā tau mahāghorau dānavau madhukaiṭabhau 
bodhayāmasatus tūrṇaṃ śayānaṃ keśavaṃ nṛpa ।। 

yuddhārtham āgatāv atra tvayā saha mahāmate 
āvayor dehi saṃgrāmaṃ yudhyasvotthāya sāṃpratam ।। 

ityukto bhagavāṃs tābhyāṃ devadevo nṛpottama 
tatheti coktvā tau devaḥ śārṅgaṃ sajjam athākarot ।। 

jyāghoṣatalaghoṣeṇa śaṅkhaśabdena mādhavaḥ 
khaṃ diśaḥ pradiśaś caiva pūrayāmasa līlayā ।। 

tau ca rājan mahāvīryau jyāghoṣaṃ cakratus tadā 
yuyudhāte mahāghorau hariṇā madhukaiṭabhau ।। 

kṛṣṇaś ca yuyudhe tābhyāṃ līlayā jagataḥ patiḥ 
samaṃ yuddhaṃ abhūd evaṃ teṣām astrāṇi muñcatām ।। 

keśavaḥ śārṅganirmuktaiḥ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ 
tāni śastrāṇi sarvāṇi ciccheda tilaśas tadā ।। 

tau yuddhvā suciraṃ tena dānavau madhukaiṭabhau 
hatau śārṅgavinirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ kṛṣṇena durmadau ।। 

tayos tu medasā rājan viṣṇunā kalpitā mahī 
medinīti tataḥ saṃjñām avāpeyaṃ vasuṃdharā ।। 

evaṃ kṛṣṇaprasādena vedāṃl labdhvā prajāpatiḥ 
prajāḥ sasarja bhūpāla vedadṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। 

ya idaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ prādurbhāvaṃ harer nṛpa 
vasitvā candrasadane vedavid brāhmaṇo bhavet ।। 

mātsyaṃ vapus tan mahad adritulyaṃ vidyāmayaṃ lokahitāya viṣṇuḥ 
āsthāya bhīmaṃ janalokasaṃsthaiḥ stuto atha yas taṃ smara bhūmipāla ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapūrāṇe matsyaprādurbhāvo nāma saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

purā devāsure yuddhe devā daityaiḥ parājitāḥ 
sarve te śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ kṣīrābdhitanayāpatim ।। 

stotreṇa tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve samārādhya jagatpatim 
kṛtāñjalipuṭā rājan brahmādyā devatāgaṇāḥ ।। 

namas te devadevāya lokanāthāya śārṅgiṇe 
namas te padmanābhāya lokanāthāya śārṅgiṇe ।। 

namas te padmanābhāya sarvaduḥkhāpahāriṇe 
namas te viśvarūpāya sarvadevamayāya ca ।। 

madhukaiṭabhanāśāya keśavāya namo namaḥ ।। 

daityaiḥ parājitā deva vayaṃ yuddhe balānvitaiḥ 
jayopāyaṃ hi no brūhi karuṇākara te namaḥ ।। 

iti stuto tadā daivair devadevo janārdanaḥ 
tān abravīd dharir devān teṣām evāgrataḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

gatvā tatra surāḥ sarve saṃdhiṃ kuruta dānavaiḥ 
manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā netraṃ kṛtvā ca vāsukim ।। 

sarvauṣadhīḥ samānīya prakṣipyābdhau tvarānvitāḥ 
dānavaiḥ sahitā bhūtvā manthadhvaṃ kṣīrasāgaram ।। 

ahaṃ ca tatra sāhāyyaṃ kariṣyāmi divaukasaḥ 
bhaviṣyaty amṛtaṃ tatra tatpānād balavattarāḥ ।। 

bhaviṣyanti kṣaṇād devā amṛtasya prabhāvataḥ 
yūyaṃ sarve mahābhāgās tejiṣṭhā raṇavikramāḥ ।। 

indrādyās tu mahotsāhās tal labdhvāmṛtam uttamam 
tato hi dānavāñ jetuṃ samarthā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

ityuktā devadevena devāḥ sarve jagatpatim 
praṇamyāgatya nilayaṃ saṃdhiṃ kṛtvātha dānavaiḥ ।। 

kṣīrābdher manthane sarve cakrur udyogam uttamam 
balinā coddhṛto rājan mandarākhyo mahāgiriḥ ।। 

kṣīrābdhau kṣepitaś caiva tenaikena nṛpottama 
sarvauṣadhīṃś ca prakṣipya devadaityaiḥ payonidhau ।। 

vāsukiś cāgatas tatra rājan nārāyaṇājñayā 
sarve devahitārthāya viṣṇuś ca svayam āgataḥ ।। 

tatra viṣṇuṃ samāsādya tataḥ sarve surāsurāḥ 
sarve te maitrabhāvena kṣīrābdhes taṭam āśritāḥ ।। 

manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā netraṃ kṛtvātha vāsukim 
tato mathitum ārabdhaṃ nṛpate tarasāmṛtam ।। 

viṣṇunā mukhabhāge tu yojitā dānavās tadā 
devatāḥ pucchabhāge tu mathanāya niyojitāḥ ।। 

evaṃ ca mathanāt tatra mandaro adhaḥ praviśya ca 
ādhāreṇa vinā rājan taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā hariḥ ।। 

sarvalokahitārthāya kūrmarūpam ādhārayat 
ātmānaṃ saṃpraviśyātha mandarasya girer adhaḥ ।। 

praviśya dhṛtavān śailaṃ mandaraṃ madhusūdanaḥ 
upary ākrāntavān śailaṃ pṛthagrūpeṇa keśavaḥ ।। 

cakarṣa nāgarājaṃ ca devaiḥ sārdhaṃ janārdanaḥ 
surair adṛśyarūpeṇa daityamadhye janārdanaḥ 
tatas te tvarayā yuktā mamanthuḥ kṣīrasāgaram ।। 

yāvacchaktyā nṛpaśreṣṭha balavantaḥ surāsurāḥ 
mathyamānāt tatas tasmāt kṣīrābdher abhavan nṛpa ।। 

kālakūṭam iti khyātaṃ viṣam atyantaduḥsaham 
taṃ nāgā jagṛhuḥ sarve taccheṣaṃ śaṃkaro agrahīt ।। 

nārāyaṇājñayā tena nīlakaṇṭhatvam āptavān 
airāvataś ca nāgendro hariś coccaiḥśravāḥ punaḥ ।। 

dvitīyāvartanād rājann utpannāv iti naḥ śrutam 
tṛtīyāvartanād rājann apsarāś ca suśobhanā 
caturthāt parijātaś ca utpannaḥ sa mahādrumaḥ ।। 

pañcamād dhi himāṃśus tu protthitaḥ kṣīrasāgarāt 
taṃ bhavaḥ śirasā dhatte nārīvat svastikaṃ nṛpa ।। 

nānāvidhāni divyāni ratnāny ābharaṇāni ca 
kṣīrodadher utthitāś ca gandharvāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। 

etān dṛṣṭvā tathotpannān atyāścaryasamanvitān 
abhavan jātaharṣās te tatra sarve surāsurāḥ ।। 

devapakṣe tato meghāḥ svalpaṃ varṣanti saṃsthitāḥ 
kṛṣṇājñayā ca vāyuś ca sukhaṃ vāti surān prati ।। 

viṣaniḥśvāsavātena vāsukeś cāpare hatāḥ 
nistejaso abhavan daityā nirvīryāś ca mahāmate ।। 

tataḥ śrīr utthitā tasmāt kṣīrodād dhṛtapaṅkajā 
vibhrājamānā rājendra diśaḥ sarvāḥ svatejasā ।। 

tatas tīrthodakaiḥ snātā divyavastrair alaṃkṛtā 
divyagandhānuliptāṅgī sumanobhiḥ subhūṣaṇaih ।। 

devapakṣaṃ samāsādya sthitvā kṣaṇam ariṃdama 
harivakṣaḥsthalaṃ prāptā tataḥ sā kamalālayā ।। 

tato amṛtaghaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ dugdhvā tu payaso nidheḥ 
dhanvantariḥ samuttasthau tataḥ prītāḥ surā nṛpa ।। 

daityāḥ śriyā parityaktā duḥkhitās te abhavan nṛpa 
nītvāmṛtaghaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ te ca jagmur yathāsukham ।। 

tataḥ strīrūpam akarod viṣṇur devahitāya vai 
ātmānaṃ nṛpaśārdūla sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।। 

tato jagāma bhagavān strīrūpeṇāsurān prati 
divyarūpāṃ tu tāṃ dṛṣṭvā mohitās te suradviṣaḥ ।। 

sudhāpūrṇaghaṭaṃ te tu mohaiḥ saṃsthāpya sattama 
kāmena pīḍitā hy āsann asurās tatra tatkṣaṇāt ।। 

mohayitvā tu tān evam asurān avanīpate 
amṛtaṃ tu samādāya devebhyaḥ pradadau hariḥ ।। 

tat pītvā tu tato devā devadevaprasādataḥ 
balavanto mahāvīryā raṇe jagmus tato asurān ।। 

jitvā raṇe asurān devāḥ svāni rājyāni cakrire 
etat te kathitaṃ rājan prādurbhāvo harer ayam ।। 

kūrmākhyaḥ puṇyado nṝṇāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ paṭhatām api 
āviskṛtaṃ kaurmam anantavarcasaṃ nārāyaṇenādbhutakarmakāriṇā 
divaukasānāṃ tu hitāya kevalaṃ rūpaṃ paraṃ pāvanam eva kīrtitam ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe kūrmaprādurbhāvo nāmāṣṭatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

ataḥparaṃ hareḥ puṇyaṃ prādurbhāvaṃ narādhipa 
vārāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu ।। 

ābantapralaye prāpte brahmaṇas tu dinakṣaye 
trailokyam akhilaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhanty ambhāṃsi sattama ।। 

trailokye akhilasattvāni yāni rājendra tāni vai 
grastvā viṣṇus tataḥ śete tasminn ekārṇave jale ।। 

anantabhogaśayane sahasraphaṇaśobhite 
rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ brahmarūpī jagatpatiḥ ।। 

diteḥ putro mahān āsīt kaśyapād iti naḥ śrutam 
hiraṇyākṣa iti khyāto mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। 

pātāle nivasan daityo devān uparurodha saḥ 
yajvinām apākārāya yatate sa tu bhūtale ।। 

atha bhūmyupari sthitvā martyā yakṣyanti devatāḥ 
tena teṣāṃ balaṃ vīryaṃ tejaś cāpi bhaviṣyati ।। 

iti matvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ kṛtasargaṃ tu brahmaṇā 
bhūmer yā dhāraṇāśaktis tāṃ nītvā sa mahāsuraḥ ।। 

viveśa toyamadhye tu rasātalatalaṃ nṛpa 
vinā śaktyā ca jagatī praviveśa rasātalam ।। 

nidrāvasāne sarvātmā kva sthitā medinīti vai 
saṃcintya jñātvā yogena rasātalatalaṃ gatām ।। 

atha vedamayaṃ rūpaṃ vārāhaṃ vapur āsthitam 
vedapādaṃ yūpadaṃṣṭraṃ ketuvaktraṃ narādhipa ।। 

vyūḍhoraskaṃ mahābāhu pṛthuvaktraṃ narādhipa 
agnijihvaṃ srucaṃ tuṇḍaṃ candrārkanayanaṃ mahat ।। 

pūrteṣṭadharmaśravaṇaṃ divyaṃ tat sāmaniḥsvanam 
prāgvaṃśakāyaṃ havirnāsaṃ kuśadarbhatanūruham ।। 

sarvavedamayaṃ tac ca puṇyasūktamahāsaṭam 
nakṣatratārāhāraṃ ca pralayāvartabhūṣaṇam ।। 

itthaṃ kṛtvā tu vārāhaṃ praviveśa vṛṣākapiḥ 
rasātalaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha sanakādyair abhiṣṭutaḥ ।। 

praviśya ca hiraṇyākṣaṃ yuddhe jitvā vṛṣākapiḥ 
daṃṣṭrāgreṇa tataḥ pṛthvīm samuddhṛtya rasātalāt ।। 

stūyamāno amaragaṇaiḥ sthāpayāmasa pūrvavat 
saṃsthāpya parvatān sarvān yathāsthānam akalpayat ।। 

vihāya rūpaṃ vārāhaṃ tīrthe koketi viśrute 
vaiṣṇavānāṃ hitārthāya kṣetraṃ tad guptam uttamam ।। 

brahmarūpaṃ samāsthāya punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ cakāra saḥ 
viṣṇuḥ pāti jagat sarvam evaṃbhūto yuge yuge 
hanti cānte jagat sarvaṃ rudrarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। 

vedāntavedyaḥ puruṣo vṛṣākapeḥ kathām imāṃ yaś ca śṛṇoti mānavaḥ 
dṛḍhāṃ matiṃ yajñatanau viveśya vai vihāya pāpaṃ ca naro hariṃ vrajet ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe vārāhaprādurbhāvo nāma ekonacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

vārāhaḥ kathito hy evaṃ prādurbhāvo hares tava 
sāṃprataṃ nārasiṃhaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi nibodha me ।। 

diteḥ putro mahān āsīd dhiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā 
tapas tepe nirāhāro bahuvarṣasahasrakam ।। 

tapatas tasya saṃtuṣṭo brahmā taṃ prāha dānavam 
varaṃ varaya daityendra yas te manasi vartate ।।
