yogābhyāsaratasyeha naśyeyuḥ pātakāni ca 
tasmād yogaparo bhūtvā dhyāyen nityaṃ kriyāntare ।। 

prāṇāyāmena vacanaṃ pratyāhāreṇa cendriyam 
dhāraṇābhir vaśīkṛtya punar durdharṣaṇaṃ manaḥ ।। 

ekaṃ kāraṇam ānandabodhaṃ ca tam anāmayam 
sukṣmāt sūkṣmataraṃ dhyāyej jagadādhāram acyutam ।। 

ātmānam aravindasthaṃ taptacāmīkaraprabham 
rahasy ekāntam āsīta dhyāyed ātmahṛdi sthitam ।। 

yaḥ sarvaprāṇacittajño yaḥ sarveṣāṃ hṛdi sthitaḥ 
yaś ca sarvajanair jñeyaḥ so aham asmīti cintayet ।। 

ātmalābhasukhaṃ yāvat tāvad dhyānam udāhṛtam 
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ karma tattadūrdhvaṃ samācaret ।। 

yathāśvā rathahīnāś ca rathāś cāśvair vinā yathā 
evaṃ tapaś ca vidyā ca ubhāv api tapasvinaḥ ।। 

yathānnaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ madhu cānnena saṃyutam 
evaṃ tapaś ca vidyā ca saṃyukte bheṣajaṃ mahat ।। 

dvābhyām eva hi pakṣābhyāṃ yathā vai pakṣiṇāṃ gatiḥ 
tathaiva jñānakarmabhyāṃ prāpyate brahma śāśvatam ।। 

vidyātapobhyāṃ saṃpanno brāhmaṇo yogatatparaḥ 
dehadvandvaṃ vihāyāśu mukto bhavati bandhanāt ।। 

na devayānamārgeṇa yāvat prāptaṃ paraṃ padam 
na tāvad dehaliṅgasya vināśo vidyate kvacit ।। 

mayā vaḥ kathitaḥ sarvo varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ 
saṃkṣepeṇa dvijaśreṣṭhā dharmas teṣāṃ sanātanaḥ ।। 

śrutvaivam ṛṣayo dharmaṃ svargamokṣaphalapradam 
praṇamya tam ṛṣiṃ jagmur muditās te svam ālayam ।। 

dharmaśāstram idaṃ yas tu hārītamukhaniḥsṛtam 
śrutvā ca kurute dharmaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

mukhajasya tu yat karma karma yad bāhujasya tu 
ūrujasya tu yat karma pādajasya tathā nṛpa ।। 

svaṃ svaṃ karma prakurvāṇā viprādyā yānti sadgatim 
anyathā vartamāno hi sadyaḥ patati yāty adhaḥ ।। 

yasya ye abhihitā dharmāḥ sa tu tais taiḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
tasmāt svadharmaṃ kurvīta nityam evam anāpadi ।। 

caturvarṇāś ca rājendra catvāraś cāpi cāśramāḥ 
svadharmaṃ ye anutiṣṭhanti te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

svadharmeṇa yathā nṛṇāṃ narasiṃhaḥ pratuṣyati 
varṇadharmānusāreṇa narasiṃhaṃ tathārcayet ।। 

utpannavairāgyabalena yogād dhyāyet paraṃ brahma sadā kriyāvān 
satyātmakaṃ citsukharūpam ādyaṃ vihāya dehaṃ padam eti viṣṇoḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe yogādhyāyo nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

varṇānām āśramāṇāṃ ca kathitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tava 
bhūyaḥ kathaya rājendra śuśrūṣā tatra kā nṛpa ।। 

snātvā veśmani deveśam arcayed acyutaṃ tv iti 
tvayoktaṃ mama viprendra tat kathaṃ pūjanaṃ bhavet ।। 

yair mantrair arcyate viṣṇur yeṣu sthāneṣu vai mune 
tāni sthānāni tān mantrāṃs tvam ācakṣva mahāmune ।। 

arcanaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ 
yat kṛtvā munayaḥ sarve paraṃ nirvāṇam āpnuyuḥ ।। 

agnau kriyāvatāṃ devo hṛdi devo manīṣiṇām 
pratimāsv alpabuddhīnāṃ yogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ ।। 

ato agnau hṛdaye sūrye sthaṇḍile pratimāsu ca 
eteṣu ca hareḥ samyag arcanaṃ munibhiḥ smṛtam ।। 

tasya sarvamayatvāc ca sthaṇḍile pratimāsu ca 
ānuṣṭubhasya sūktasya viṣṇus tasya ca devatā ।। 

puruṣo yo jagadbījaṃ ṛṣir nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
dadyāt puruṣasūktena yaḥ puṣpāṇy apa eva ca ।। 

arcitaṃ syāj jagat sarvaṃ tena vai sacarācaram 
ādyayāvāhayed devam ṛcā tu puruṣottamam ।। 

dvitīyayāsanaṃ dadyāt pādyaṃ dadyāt tṛtīyayā 
caturthyārghyaḥ pradātavyaḥ pañcamyācamanīyakam ।। 

ṣaṣṭhyā snānaṃ prakurvīta saptamyā vastram eva ca 
yajñopavītam aṣṭamyā navamyā gandham eva ca ।। 

daśamyā puṣpadānaṃ syād ekādaśyā ca dhūpakam 
dvādaśyā ca tathā dīpaṃ trayodaśyārcanaṃ tathā ।। 

caturdaśyā stutiṃ kṛtvā pañcadaśyā pradakṣiṇam 
ṣoḍaśyodvāsanaṃ kuryāc cheṣakarmāṇi pūrvavat ।। 

snānaṃ vastraṃ ca naivedyaṃ dadyād ācanamīyakam 
ṣaṇmāsāt siddhim āpnoti devadevaṃ samarcayan ।। 

saṃvatsareṇa tenaiva sāyujyam adhigachati 
haviṣāgnau jale puṣpair dhyānena hṛdaye harim ।। 

arcanti sūrayo nityaṃ japena ravimaṇḍale 
ādityamaṇḍale divyaṃ devadevam anāmayam 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ dhyātvā viṣṇum upāsate ।। 

dhyeyaḥ sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī nārāyaṇaḥ sarasijāsanasaṃniviṣṭaḥ 
keyūravān makarakuṇḍalavān kirīṭī hārī hiraṇmayavapur dhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ ।। 

etat paṭhan kevalam eva sūktaṃ dine dine bhāvitaviṣṇubuddhiḥ 
sa sarvapāpaṃ pravihāya vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ prayāty acyutatuṣṭikṛn naraḥ ।। 

patreṣu puṣpeṣu phaleṣu toyeṣv akrītalabhyeṣu sadaiva satsu 
bhaktyaikalabhye puruṣe purāṇe muktyai kimarthaṃ kriyate na yatnaḥ ।। 

ity evam uktaḥ puruṣasya viṣṇor arcāvidhis te adya mayā nṛpendra 
anena nityaṃ kuru viṣṇupūjāṃ prāptuṃ tadiṣṭaṃ yadi vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe viṣṇor arcāvidhir nāma dviṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

satyam uktaṃ tvayā brahman vaidikaḥ paramo vidhiḥ 
viṣṇor devātidevasya pūjanaṃ prati me adhunā ।। 

anena vidhinā brahman pūjyate madhusūdanaḥ 
vedajñair eva nānyais tu tasmāt sarvahitaṃ vada ।। 

aṣṭākṣareṇa deveśaṃ narasiṃham anāmayam 
gandhapuṣpādibhir nityam arcayed acyutaṃ naraḥ ।। 

rājann aṣṭākṣaro mantraḥ sarvapāpaharaḥ paraḥ 
samastayajñaphaladaḥ sarvaśāntikaraḥ śubhaḥ ।। 

oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya ।

gandhapuṣpādisakalam anena vai nivedayet 
anenābhyarcito devaḥ prīto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ।। 

kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantraiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhir vrataiḥ 
oṃ namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। 

imaṃ mantraṃ japed yas tu śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇusāyujyam āpnuyāt ।। 

sarvatīrthaphalaṃ hy etat sarvatīrthavaraṃ nṛpa 
harer arcanam avyagraṃ sarvayajñaphalaṃ nṛpa ।। 

tasmāt kuru nṛpaśreṣṭha pratimādiṣu cārcanam dānāni vipramukhebhyaḥ prayaccha vidhinā nṛpa 
evaṃ kṛte nṛpaśreṣṭha narasiṃhaprasādataḥ prāpnoti vaiṣṇavaṃ tejo yat kāṅkṣanti mumukṣavaḥ ।। 

purā puraṃdaro rājan strītvaṃ prāpto apadharmataḥ 
tṛṇabindumuneḥ śāpān mukto hy aṣṭākṣarāj japāt ।। 

etat kathaya bhūdeva devendrasyāghamocanam 
ko apadharmaḥ kathaṃ strītvaṃ prāpto me vada kāraṇam ।। 

rājendra mahad ākhyānaṃ śṛṇu kautūhalānvitam 
viṣṇubhaktiprajananaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ paṭhatām idam ।। 

purā puraṃdarasyaiva devarājyaṃ prakurvataḥ 
vairāgyasyāpi jananaṃ saṃbhūtaṃ bāhyavastuṣu ।। 

indras tadābhūd viṣamasvabhāvo rājyeṣu bhogeṣv api so apy acintayat 
dhruvaṃ virāgīkṛtamānasānāṃ svargasya rājyaṃ na ca kiṃcid eva ।। 

rājyasya sāraṃ viṣayeṣu bhogo bhogasya cānte na ca kiṃcid asti 
vimṛśya caitan munayo apy ajasraṃ mokṣādhikāraṃ paricintayanti ।। 

sadaiva bhogāya tapaḥpravṛttir bhogāvasāne hi tapo vinaṣṭam 
maitryādisaṃyogaparāṅmukhānāṃ vimuktibhājāṃ na tapo na bhogaḥ ।। 

vimṛśya caitat sa surādhinātho vimānam āruhya sakiṅkiṇīkam 
nūnaṃ harārādhanakāraṇena kailāsam abhyeti vimuktikāmaḥ ।। 

sa ekadā mānasam āgataḥ san saṃvīkṣya tāṃ yakṣapateś ca kāntām 
samarcayantīṃ girijāṅghriyugmaṃ dhvajām ivānaṅgamahārathasya ।। 

pradhānajāmbūnadaśuddhavarṇāṃ karṇāntasaṃlagnamanojñanetrām 
susūkṣmavastrāntaradṛśyagātrāṃ nīhāramadhyād iva candralekhām ।। 

tāṃ vīkṣya vīkṣaṇasahasrabhareṇa kāmaṃ kāmāṅgamohitamatir na yayau tadānīm 
dūrādhvagaṃ svagṛham etya susaṃcitārthas tasthau tadā surapatir viṣayābhilāṣī ।। 

pūrvaṃ varaṃ syāt sukule api janma tato hi sarvāṅgaśarīrarūpam 
tato dhanaṃ durlabham eva paścād dhanādhipatyaṃ sukṛtena labhyam ।। 

svargādhipatyaṃ ca mayā pralabdhaṃ tathāpi bhogāya na cāsti bhāgyam 
yaḥ svaṃ parityajya vimuktikāmas tiṣṭhāmi me durmatir asti citte ।। 

mokṣo amunā yady api mohanīyo mokṣe api kiṃ kāraṇam asti rājye 
kṣetraṃ supakvaṃ parihṛtya dvāre kiṃ nāma cāraṇyakṛṣiṃ karoti ।। 

saṃsāraduḥkhopahatā narā ye kartuṃ samarthā na ca kiṃcid eva 
akarmiṇo bhāgyavivarjitāś ca vāñchanti te mokṣapathaṃ vimūḍhāḥ ।। 

etad vimṛśya bahudhā matimān pravīro rūpeṇa mohitamanā dhanadāṅganāyāḥ 
sarvādhir ākulamatiḥ parimuktadhairyaḥ sasmāra māram amarādhipacakravartī ।। 

samāgato asau parimandamandaṃ kāmo atikāmākulacittavṛttiḥ 
purā maheśena kṛtāṅganāśo dhairyāl layaṃ gacchati ko viśaṅkaḥ ।। 

ādiśyatāṃ nātha yad asti kāryaṃ ko nāma te saṃprati śatrubhūtaḥ 
śīghraṃ samādeśaya mā vilambaṃ tasyāpadaṃ saṃprati bho diśāmi ।। 

śrutvā tadā tasya vaco abhirāmaṃ manogataṃ tat paramaṃ tutoṣa 
niṣpannam arthaṃ sahasaiva matvā jagāda vākyaṃ sa vihasya vīraḥ ।। 

rudro api yenārdhaśarīramātraś cakre apy anaṅgatvam upāgatena 
soḍhuṃ samartho atha paro api loke ko nāma te māra śarābhighātam ।। 

ekāgracittā girijārcane api yā mohayaty eva mamātra cittam 
etām anaṅgāyatalocanākhyāṃ madaṅgasaṅgaikarasāṃ vidhehi ।। 

sa evam uktaḥ suravallabhena svakāryabhāvādhikagauraveṇa 
saṃdhāya bāṇaṃ kusumāyudho api sasmāra māraḥ parimohanaṃ sudhīḥ ।। 

saṃmohitā puṣpaśareṇa bālā kāmena kāmaṃ madavihvalāṅgī 
vihāya pūjāṃ hasate sureśaṃ kaḥ kāmakodaṇḍaravaṃ saheta ।। 

vilolanetre ayi kāsi bāle surādhipo vākyam idaṃ jagāda 
saṃmohayantīva manāṃsi puṃsāṃ kasyeha kāntā vada puṇyabhājaḥ ।। 

uktāpi bālā madavihvalāṅgī romāñcasaṃsvedasakampagātrā 
kṛtākulā kāmaśilīmukhena sagadgadaṃ vākyam uvāca mandam ।। 

kāntā dhaneśasya ca yakṣakanyā prāptā ca gaurīcaraṇārcanāya 
prabrūhi kāryaṃ ca tavāsti nātha kas tvaṃ vades tiṣṭhasi kāmarūpaḥ ।। 

sā tvaṃ samāgaccha bhajasva māṃ cirān madaṅgasaṅgotsukatāṃ vrajāśu 
tvayā vinā jīvitam apy analpaṃ svargasya rājyaṃ mama niṣphalaṃ syāt ।। 

uktā ca saivaṃ madhuraṃ ca tena kandarpasaṃtāpitacārudehā 
vimānam āruhya calatpatākaṃ sureśakaṇṭhagrahaṇaṃ cakāra ।। 

jagāma śīghraṃ sa hi nākanāthaḥ sākaṃ tayā mandarakandarāsu 
adṛṣṭadevāsurasaṃcarāsu vicitraratnāṅkurabhāsurāsu ।। 

reme tayā sākam udāravīryaś citraṃ suraiśvaryagatādaro api 
svayaṃ ca yasyā laghupuṣpaśayyāṃ cakāra cāturyanidhiḥ sakāmaḥ ।। 

jātaḥ kṛtārtho amaravṛndanāthaḥ sakāmabhogeṣu sadā vidagdhaḥ 
mokṣādhikaṃ sneharasātimṛṣṭaṃ parāṅganāliṅganasaṅgasaukhyam ।। 

athāgatā yakṣapateḥ samīpaṃ nāryo anuvarjyaiva ca citrasenām 
sasaṃbhramāḥ saṃbhramakhinnagātrāḥ sagadgadaṃ procur asāhasajñāḥ ।। 

nūnaṃ samākarṇaya yakṣanātha vimānam āropya jagāma kaścit 
saṃvīkṣamāṇaḥ kakubho api kāntāṃ vigṛhya vegād iha so api taskaraḥ ।। 

vaco niśamyātha dhanādhinātho viṣopamaṃ jātamaṣīnibhānanaḥ 
jagāda bhūyo na ca kiṃcid eva babhūva vai vṛkṣa ivāgnidagdhaḥ ।। 

vijñāpitārtho varakanyakābhir yaś citrasenāsahacāriṇībhiḥ 
mohāpanodāya matiṃ dadhānaḥ sa kaṇṭhakubjo api samājagāma ।। 

śrutvāgataṃ vīkṣya sa rājarāja unmīlitākṣo vacanaṃ jagāda 
viniḥśvasan gāḍhasakampagātraḥ svasthaṃ mano apy āśu vidhāya dīnaḥ ।। 

tad yauvanaṃ yad yuvatīvinodo dhanaṃ tu caitat svajanopayogi 
taṃ jīvitaṃ yat kriyate sudharmas tad ādhipatyaṃ yadi naṣṭavigraham ।। 

dhiṅ me dhanaṃ jīvitam atyanalpaṃ rājyaṃ bṛhat saṃprati guhyakānām 
viśāmi cāgniṃ na ca veda kaścit parābhavo astīti ca ko mṛtānām ।। 

pārśve sthitasyāpi ca jīvito me gatā taḍāgaṃ girijārcanāya 
hṛtā ca kenāpi vayaṃ na vidmo dhruvaṃ na tasyāsti bhayaṃ ca mṛtyoḥ ।। 

jagāda vākyaṃ sa ca kaṇṭhakubjo mohāpanodāya vibhoḥ sa mantrī 
ākarṇyatāṃ nātha na cāsti yogyaḥ kāntāviyoge nijadehaghātaḥ ।। 

ekā purā rāmavadhūr hṛtā ca niśācareṇāpi mṛto na so api 
anekaśaḥ santi tavātra nāryaḥ ko nāma citte kriyate viṣādaḥ ।। 

vimucya śokaṃ kuru vikrame matiṃ dhairyaṃ samālambaya yakṣarāja 
bhṛśaṃ na jalpanti rudanti sādhavaḥ parābhavaṃ bāhyakṛtaṃ sahante ।। 

kṛtaṃ hi kāryaṃ guru darśayanti sahāyavān vittapa kātaro asi kim 
sahāyakāryaṃ kurute hi saṃprati svayaṃ hi yasyāvarajo vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। 

vibhīṣaṇo me pratipakṣabhūto dāyādabhāvaṃ na vimuñcatīti 
dhruvaṃ prasannā na bhavanti durjanāḥ kṛtopakārā harivajraniṣṭhurāḥ ।। 

na copakārair na guṇair na sauhṛdaiḥ prasādam āyāti mano hi gotriṇaḥ 
uvāca vākyaṃ sa ca kaṇṭhakubjo yuktaṃ tvayoktaṃ ca dhanādhinātha ।। 

parasparaṃ ghnanti ca te viruddhās tathāpi loke na parābhavo asti 
parābhavaṃ nānyakṛtaṃ sahante noṣṇaṃ jalaṃ jvālayate tṛṇāni ।। 

tasmāt samāgaccha dhanādhinātha pārśvaṃ na vegena vibhīṣaṇasya 
svabāhuvīryārjitavittabhogināṃ svabandhuvargeṣu hi ko virodhaḥ ।। 

ityuktaḥ sa tadā tena kaṇṭhakubjena mantriṇā 
vibhīṣaṇasya sāmīpyaṃ jagāmāśu vicārayan ।। 

tato laṅkādhipaḥ śrutvā bāndhavaṃ pūrvajaṃ tadā 
prāptaṃ pratyājagāmāśu vinayena samanvitaḥ ।। 

tato vibhīṣaṇo dṛṣṭvā tadā dīnaṃ ca bāndhavam 
saṃtaptamānaso bhūpa jagādedaṃ vaco mahat ।। 

kathaṃ dīno asi yakṣeśa kiṃ kaṣṭaṃ tava cetasi 
nivedayādhunāsmākaṃ niścayān mārjayāmi tat ।। 

tadaikāntaṃ samāsādya kathayāmasa vedanām ।। b

gṛhītā kiṃ svayaṃ yātā nihatā kenacid dviṣā ।। d

bhrātaḥ kāntāṃ na paśyāmi citrasenāṃ manoramām 
etad bandho mahat kaṣṭaṃ mama nārīsamudbhavam ।। 

prāṇān vai ghātayiṣyāmi anāsādya ca vallabhām ।। b

ānayiṣyāmi te kāntāṃ yatra tatra sthitāṃ vibho ।। d

kaḥ samartho adhunāsmākaṃ hartuṃ nātha tṛṇasya ca 
tato vibhīṣaṇas tatra nāḍījaṅghāṃ niśācarīm ।। 

bhṛśaṃ saṃjalpayāmasa nānāmāyāgarīyasīm 
dhanadasya ca yā kāntā citrasenāvidhānataḥ ।। 

sā ca kena hṛtā loke manase sarasi sthitā 
tāṃ ca jānīhi saṃvīkṣya devarājādiveśmasu ।। 

tato niśācarī bhūpa kṛtvā māyāmayaṃ vapuḥ 
jagāma tridivaṃ śīghraṃ devarājādiveśmasu ।। 

yayā dṛṣṭyā kṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭo mohaṃ yāsyati copalaḥ 
yasyāḥ samaṃ dhruvaṃ rūpaṃ vidyate na carācare ।। 

etasminn eva kāle ca devarājo api bhūpate 
saṃprāpto mandarāc chīghraṃ preritaś citrasenayā ।। 

grahītuṃ divyapuṣpāṇi nandanaprabhavāṇi ca 
tatra paśyan sa tāṃ tanvīṃ nijasthāne sabhāgatām ।। 

atīvarūpasaṃpannāṃ gītagānaparāyaṇām 
tāṃ vīkṣya devarājo api sa kāmavaśago abhavat ।। 

tataḥ saṃprerayāmasa devavaidyau surādhipaḥ 
tasyāḥ pārśve samānetuṃ dhruvaṃ cāntaḥpure tadā ।। 

devavaidyau tadāgatya jalpataś cāgrataḥ sthitau 
āgaccha bhava tanvaṅgi devarājasamīpagā ।। 

ityuktā sā tadā tābhyāṃ jagāda madhurākṣaram ।। b

devarājaḥ svayaṃ yan me pārśvaṃ cātrāgamiṣyati ।। d

tasya vācyaṃ ca kartavyaṃ nānyathā sarvathā mayā 
tau tadā vāsavaṃ gatvā ūcatur vacanaṃ śubham ।। 

samādeśaya tanvaṅgi kiṃ kartavyaṃ mayādhunā 
sarvadā dāsabhūtas te yācase tad dadāmy aham ।। 

yācitaṃ yadi me nātha dāsyasīti na saṃśayaḥ 
tato ahaṃ vaśagā deva bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

adya tvaṃ darśayāsmākaṃ sarvaḥ kāntāparigrahaḥ 
mama rūpasamā rāmā kāntā te cāsti vā na vā ।। 

tayā cokte ca vacane sa bhūyo vāsavo avadat 
darśayiṣyāmi sarvaṃ te devi kāntāparigraham ।। 

sa sarvaṃ darśayāmasa vāsavo antaḥpuraṃ tadā 
tato jagāda bhūyaḥ sa kiṃcid gūḍhaṃ mama sthitam ।। 

vimucyaikāṃ ca yuvatīṃ sarvaṃ te darśitaṃ mayā ।। b

sā rāmā mandare cāsti avijñātā surāsuraiḥ ।। d

tāṃ ca te darśayiṣyāmi nākhyeyaṃ kasyacit tvayā 
tataḥ sa devarājo api tayā sārdhaṃ ca bhūpate ।। 

gacchann evāmbare bhūpa mandaraṃ prati bhūdharam 
tasya vai gacchamānasya vimānenārkavarcasā ।। 

darśanaṃ nāradasyāpi tasya jātaṃ tadāmbare 
taṃ vīkṣya nāradaṃ vīro lajjamāno api vāsavaḥ ।। 

namaskṛtya jagādoccaiḥ kva yāsyasi mahāmune 
tataḥ kṛtāśīḥ sa munir avadat trideveśvaram ।। 

gacchāmi mānase snātuṃ devarāja sukhī bhava 
nāḍījaṅghe asti kuśalaṃ rākṣasānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 

vibhīṣaṇo api te bhrātā sukhī tiṣṭhati sarvadā 
evam uktā ca muninā sā kṛṣṇavadanābhavat ।। 

vismito devarājo api chalito duṣṭayānayā 
nārado api gataḥ snātuṃ kailāse mānasaṃ saraḥ ।। 

indras tāṃ hantukāmo api āgacchan mandarācalam 
yatrāśramo asti vai nūnaṃ tṛṇabindor mahātmanaḥ ।। 

kṣaṇaṃ viśramya tatraiva dhṛtvā keśeṣu rākṣasīm 
hantum icchati deveśo nāḍījaṅghāṃ niśācarīm ।। 

tāvat tatra samāyātas tṛṇabindur nijāśramāt 
dhṛtā krandati sā rājann indreṇāpi niśācarī ।। 

mā māṃ rakṣati puṇyātmā hanyamānāṃ ca sāṃpratam 
tadāgatya muniśreṣṭhas tṛṇabindur mahātapāḥ ।। 

jagāda purataḥ sthitvā muñcemāṃ mahilāṃ vane 
jalpaty evaṃ munau tasmin mahendreṇa niśācarī ।। 

vajreṇa nihatā bhūyaḥ kopayuktena cetasā 
sa cukopa muniśreṣṭhaḥ prekṣamāṇo muhur muhuḥ ।। 

yad eṣā yuvatī duṣṭa nihatā me tapovane 
tatas tvaṃ mama śāpena niścayāt strī bhaviṣyasi ।। 

eṣā nātha mahāduṣṭā rākṣasī nihatā mayā 
ahaṃ svāmī surāṇāṃ ca śāpaṃ mā dehi me adhunā ।। 

nūnaṃ tapovane asmākaṃ duṣṭās tiṣṭhanti sādhavaḥ 
mamātra tapaso bhāvān na nighnanti parasparam ।। 

ityukto hi tadā cendraḥ prāptaḥ strītvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
jagāma tridivaṃ bhūpa hataśaktiparākramaḥ ।। 

nāsīno hi bhavaty eva sarvadā devasaṃsadi 
devā duḥkhaṃ samāpannā dṛṣṭvā strītvaṃ gataṃ harim ।। 

tato devagaṇāḥ sarve vāsavena samanvitāḥ 
jagmuś ca brahmasadanaṃ tathā dīnā śacī tadā ।। 

brahmā bhagnasamādhiś ca tāvat tatraiva saṃsthitāḥ 
devā ūcuś ca te sarve vāsavena samanvitāḥ ।। 

tṛṇabindor muneḥ śāpād yātaḥ strītvaṃ surādhipaḥ 
sa muniḥ kopavān brahman naiva gacchaty anugraham ।। 

svakarmaṇopayāto sau strītvaṃ strīvadhakāraṇāt ।। 

cakāra durnayaṃ devā devarājo api durmadaḥ 
jahāra citrasenāṃ ca suguptāṃ dhanadāṅganām ।। 

tathā jaghāna yuvatīṃ tṛṇabindos tapovane 
tena karmavipākena strībhāvaṃ vāsavo gataḥ ।। 

yad asau kṛtavāñ śaṃbhor durnayaṃ nātha durmatiḥ 
tat sarvaṃ sādhayiṣyāmo vayaṃ śacyā samanvitāḥ ।। 

kāntā dhanādhināthasya gūḍhā tiṣṭhati yā vibho 
tāṃ ca tasmai pradāsyāmaḥ sarve kṛtvā parāṃ matim ।। 

trayodaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ devarājaḥ śacīyutaḥ 
nandane cārcanaṃ kartā sarvadā yakṣarakṣasām ।। 

tataḥ śacī tadā gūḍhaṃ citrasenāṃ vigṛhya ca 
mumoca yakṣabhavanaṃ priyakaṣṭānuvartinīm ।। 

etasminn antare dūto akāle laṅkāṃ samāgataḥ 
dhaneśaṃ kathayāmasa citrasenāsamāgamam ।। 

śacyā sākaṃ samāyātā tava kāntā dhanādhipa 
sakhīṃ svām atulāṃ prāpya caritārthā babhūva sā ।। 

dhaneśo api kṛtārtho abhūj jagāma nijaveśmani 
patihīnā yathā nārī nāthahīnaṃ yathā balam 
gokulaṃ kṛṣṇahīnaṃ tu tathendreṇāmarāvatī ।। 

japaḥ kriyā tapo dānaṃ jñānaṃ tīrthaṃ ca vai prabho 
vāsavasya samākhyāhi yataḥ strītvād vimucyate ।। 

nihantuṃ na muneḥ śāpaṃ samartho ahaṃ na śaṃkaraḥ 
tīrthaṃ cānyan na paśyāmi muktvaikaṃ viṣṇupūjanam ।। 

aṣṭākṣareṇa mantreṇa pūjanaṃ ca tathā japam 
karotu vidhivac chakraḥ strītvād yena ca mucyate ।। 

ekāgramanasā śakra snātvā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ 
oṃ namo narāyaṇāyeti japa tvam ātmaśuddhaye ।। 

lakṣadvaye kṛte jāpye strībhāvān mucyase hare 
iti śrutvā tathākārṣīd brahmoktaṃ vacanaṃ hariḥ 
strībhāvāc ca vinirmuktas tadā viṣṇoḥ prasādataḥ ।। 

iti te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ viṣṇumāhātmyam uttamam 
mayā bhṛguniyuktena kuru sarvam atandritaḥ ।। 

śṛṇvanti ye viṣṇukathām akalmaṣā vīryaṃ hi viṣṇo akhilakāraṇasya 
te muktapāpāḥ paradāragāmino viśanti viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ dhruvam ।। 

iti sambodhitas tena mārkaṇḍeyena pārthivaḥ 
narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya prāptavān vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।। 

etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bharadvāja mune mayā 
sahasrānīkacaritaṃ kim anyat kathayāmi te ।। 

kathām imāṃ yas tu śṛṇoti mānavaḥ purātanīṃ sarvavimuktidāṃ ca 
saṃprāpya sa jñānam atīva nirmalaṃ tenaiva viṣṇuṃ pratipadyate janaḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite aṣṭākṣaramantrakathanaṃ nāma triṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

satyaṃ kecit praśaṃsanti tapaḥ śaucaṃ tathāpare 
sāṃkhyaṃ kecit praśaṃsanti yogam anye pracakṣate ।। 

jñānaṃ kecit praśaṃsanti samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanāḥ 
kṣamāṃ kecit praśaṃsanti tathaiva ca dayārjavam ।। 

kecid dānaṃ praśaṃsanti kecid āhuḥ paraṃ śubham 
samyagjñānaṃ paraṃ kecit kecid vairāgyam uttamam ।। 

agniṣṭomādikarmāṇi tathā kecit paraṃ viduḥ 
ātmadhyānaṃ paraṃ kecit sāṃkhyatattvārthavedinaḥ ।। 

dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ caturṇām iha kevalam 
upāyaḥ padabhedena bahudhaivaṃ pracakṣyate ।। 

evaṃ cāvasthite loke kṛtyākṛtyavidhau narāḥ 
vyāmoham eva gacchanti vimuktāḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ ।। 

yad eteṣu paraṃ kṛtyam anuṣṭheyaṃ mahātmabhiḥ 
vaktum arhasi sarvajña mama sarvārthasādhakam ।। 

śrūyatām idam atyantaṃ gūḍhaṃ saṃsāramocanam 
atraivodāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।। 

puṇḍarīkasya saṃvādaṃ devarṣer nāradasya ca 
brāhmaṇaḥ śrutasaṃpannaḥ puṇḍarīko mahāmatiḥ ।। 

āśrame prathame tiṣṭhan gurūṇāṃ vaśagaḥ sadā 
jitendriyo jitakrodhaḥ saṃdhyopāsanadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। 

vedavedāṅganipuṇaḥ śāstreṣu ca vicakṣaṇaḥ 
samidbhiḥ sādhuyatnena sāyaṃ prātar hutāśanam ।। 

dhyātvā yajñapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ samyag ārādhayan vibhum 
tapassvādhyāyanirataḥ sākṣād brahmasuto yathā ।। 

udakendhanapuṣpārthair asakṛt tarpayan gurūn 
mātāpitṛbhyāṃ śuśrūṣur bhikṣāhārī janapriyaḥ ।। 

brahmavidyām adhīyāṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaḥ tasya sarvārthabhūtasya saṃsāre atyantaniḥspṛhā 
buddhir āsīn mahārāja saṃsārārṇavatāraṇī pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva bhrātṛn atha pitāmahān ।। 

pitṛvyān mātulāṃś caiva sakhīn saṃbandhibāndhavān 
parityajya mahodāras tṛṇānīva yathāsukham ।। 

vicacāra mahīm etāṃ śākamūlaphalāśanaḥ 
anityaṃ yauvanaṃ rūpam āyuṣyaṃ dravyasaṃcayam ।। 

iti saṃcintyamānena trailokyaṃ loṣṭhavat smṛtam 
purāṇoditamārgeṇa sarvatīrthāni vai mune ।। 

gamiṣyāmi yathākālam iti niścitamānasaḥ 
gaṅgāṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva gomatīm atha gaṇḍakīm ।। 

śatadrūṃ ca payoṣṇīṃ ca sarayūṃ ca sarasvatīm 
prayāgaṃ narmadāṃ caiva mahānadyo nadān api ।। 

gayāṃ ca vindhyatīrthāni himavatprabhavāṇi ca 
anyāni ca mahātejās tīrtāni sa mahāvrataḥ ।। 

saṃcacāra mahābāhur yathākālaṃ yathāvidhi 
kadācit prāptavān vīraḥ śālagrāmaṃ tapodhanaḥ ।। 

puṇḍarīko mahābhāgaḥ puṇyakarmavaśānugaḥ 
āsevyamānam ṛṣibhis tattvavidbhis tapodhanaiḥ ।। 

munīnām āśramaṃ ramyaṃ purāṇeṣu ca viśrutam 
bhūṣitaṃ cakranadyā ca cakrāṅkitaśilātalam ।। 

ramyaṃ viviktaṃ vistīrṇaṃ sadā cittaprasādakam 
kecic cakrāṅkitās tasmin prāṇinaḥ puṇyadarśanāḥ ।। 

vicaranti yathākāmaṃ puṇyatīrthaprasaṅginaḥ 
tasmin kṣetre mahāpuṇye śālagrāme mahāmatiḥ ।। 

puṇḍarīkaḥ prasannātmā tīrthāni samasevata 
snātvā devahrade tīrthe sarasvatyāṃ ca suvrataḥ ।। 

jātismaryāṃ cakrakuṇḍe cakranadyāsṛteṣv api 
tathānyāny api tīrthāni tasminn eva cacāra saḥ ।। 

tataḥ kṣetraprabhāveṇa tīrthānāṃ caiva tejasā 
manaḥ prasādam agamat tasya tasmin mahātmanaḥ ।। 

so api tīrthe viśuddhātmā dhyānayogaparāyaṇaḥ 
tatraiva siddhim ākāṅkṣan samārādhya jagatpatim ।। 

śāstroktena vidhānena bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ 
uvāsa ciram ekākī nirdvandvaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। 

śākamūlaphalāhāraḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ samadarśanaḥ 
yamaiś ca niyamaiś caiva tathā cāsanabandhanaiḥ ।। 

prāṇāyāmaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiś ca pratyāhāraiś ca saṃtataiḥ 
dhāraṇābhis tathā dhyānaiḥ samādhibhir atandritaḥ ।। 

yogābhyāsaṃ tadā samyak cakre vigatakalmaṣaḥ 
ārādhya devadeveśaṃ tadgatenāntarātmanā ।। 

puṇḍarīko mahābhāgaḥ puruṣārthaviśāradaḥ 
prasādaṃ param ākāṅkṣan viṣṇos tadgatamānasaḥ ।। 

tasya tasmin nivasataḥ śālagrāme mahātmanaḥ 
puṇḍarīkasya rājendra kālo agacchan mahāṃs tataḥ ।। 

mune kadācit taṃ deśaṃ nāradaḥ paramārthavit 
jagāma sumahātejāḥ sākṣādādityasaṃnibhaḥ ।। 

taṃ draṣṭukāmo devarṣiḥ puṇḍarīkaṃ taponidhim 
viṣṇubhaktiparītātmā vaiṣṇavānāṃ hite rataḥ ।। 

sa dṛṣṭvā nāradaṃ prāptaṃ sarvatejaḥ prabhānvitam 
mahāmatiṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvāgamaviśāradam ।। 

prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā 
arghaṃ dattvā yathāyogyaṃ praṇāmam akarot tataḥ ।। 

ko ayam atyadbhutākāras tejasvī hṛdyaveṣadhṛk 
ātodyahastaḥ sumukho jaṭāmaṇḍalabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

vivasvān atha vā vahnir indro varuṇa eva vā 
iti saṃcintayan vipraḥ papraccha paramadyutiḥ ।। 

ko bhavān iha saṃprāptaḥ kuto vā paramadyute 
tvaddarśanaṃ hy apuṇyānāṃ prāyeṇa bhuvi durlabham ।। 

nārado aham anuprāptas tvaddarśanakutūhalāt 
puṇḍarīka harer bhaktas tvādṛśaḥ satataṃ dvija ।। 

smṛtaḥ saṃbhāṣito vāpi pūjito vā dvijottama 
punāti bhagavadbhaktaś cāṇḍālo api yadṛcchayā ।। 

dāso ahaṃ vāsudevasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇah 
ityukto nāradenāsau bhaktiparyākulātmanā ।। 

provāca madhuraṃ vipras taddarśanasuvismitaḥ ।। b

dhanyo ahaṃ dehinām adya supūjyo ahaṃ surair api ।। d

kṛtārthāḥ pitaro me adya saṃprātaṃ janmaṇaḥ phalam 
anugṛhṇīṣva devarṣe tvadbhaktasya viśeṣataḥ ।। 

kiṃ kiṃ karomy ahaṃ vidvan bhrāmyamāṇaḥ svakarmabhiḥ 
kartavyaṃ paramaṃ guhyam upadeṣṭuṃ tvam arhasi ।। 

tvaṃ gatiḥ saravalokānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। b

anekānīha śāstrāṇi karmāṇi ca tathā dvija ।। d

dharmamārgāś ca bahavas tathaiva prāṇinaḥ smṛtāḥ 
vailakṣaṇyaṃ ca jagatas tasmād eva dvijottama ।। 

avyaktāj jāyate sarvaṃ sarvātmakam idaṃ jagat 
ity evaṃ prāhur apare tatraiva layam eva ca ।। 

ātmāno bahavo proktā nityāḥ sarvagatās tathā 
anyair matimatāṃ śreṣṭha tattvālokanatatparaiḥ ।। 

evamādy anusaṃcintya yathāmati yathāśrutam 
vadanti ṛṣayaḥ sarve nānāmataviśāradāḥ ।। 

śṛṇuṣvāvahito brahman kathayāmi tavānagha 
paramārtham idaṃ guhyaṃ ghorasaṃsāramocanam ।। 

anāgatam atītaṃ ca viprakṛṣṭam atīva yat 
na gṛhṇāti nṛṇāṃ dṛṣṭir vartamānārthaniścitā ।। 

śṛṇuṣvāvahitaṃ tāta kathayāmi tavānagha 
yat proktaṃ brahmaṇā pūrvaṃ pṛcchato mama suvrata ।। 

kadācid brahmalokasthaṃ padmayoniṃ pitāmaham 
praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ pṛṣṭavān aham avyayam ।। 

kiṃ taj jñānaṃ paraṃ deva kaś ca yogaḥ paras tathā 
etan me tattvataḥ sarvaṃ tvam ācakṣva pitāmaha ।। 

yaḥ paraḥ prakṛteḥ proktaḥ puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ 
sa eva sarvabhūtānāṃ nara ity abhidhīyate ।। 

narāj jātāni tattvāni nārāṇīti tato viduḥ 
tāny eva cāyanaṃ tasya tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

nārāyaṇāj jagat sarvaṃ sargakāle prajāyate 
tasminn eva punas tac ca pralaye saṃpralīyate ।। 

nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ brahma tattvaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ param 
nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ jyotir ātmā nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।। 

parād api paraś cāsau tasmān nātiparaṃ mune 
yac ca kiṃcij jagaty asmin dṛśyate śrūyate api vā ।। 

antar bahiś ca tat sarvaṃ vyāpya nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ 
evaṃ viditvā taṃ devāḥ sākāraṃ vyāharan muhuḥ ।। 

namo nārāyaṇāyeti dhyātvā cānanyamānasāḥ 
kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ ।। 

yo nityaṃ dhyāyate devaṃ nārāyaṇam ananyadhīḥ 
etaj jñānaṃ varaṃ nāto yogaś caiva paras tathā ।। 

parasparaviruddhārthaiḥ kim anyaiḥ śāstravistaraiḥ 
bahavo api yathā mārgā viśanty evaṃ mahat puram ।। 

tathā jñānāni sarvāṇi praviśanti tam īśvaram 
sa hi sarvagato devaḥ sūkṣmo avyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। 

jagadādir anādyantaḥ svayaṃbhūr bhūtabhāvanaḥ 
viṣṇur vibhur acintyātmā nityaḥ sadasadātmakaḥ ।। 

vāsudevojagadvāsaḥ purāṇaḥ kavir avyayaḥ 
yasmāt prāptaṃ sthitiṃ kṛtsnaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। 

tasmāt sa bhagavān devo viṣṇur ity abhidhīyate 
yasmād vā sarvabhūtānāṃ tattvādyānāṃ yugakṣaye ।। 

tasmin nivāsaḥ saṃsarge vāsudevas tatas tu saḥ 
tam āhuḥ puruṣaṃ kecit kecid īśvaram avyayam ।। 

vijñānamātraṃ kecic ca kecid brahma paraṃ tathā 
kecit kālam anādyantaṃ kecij jīvaṃ sanātanam ।। 

kecic ca paramātmānaṃ kecic caivam anāmayam 
kecit kṣetrajñam ity āhuḥ kecit ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ tathā ।। 

aṅguṣṭhamātraṃ kecic ca kecit padmarajoupamam 
ete cānye ca munibhiḥ saṃjñābhedāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ ।। 

śāstreṣu kathitā viṣṇor lokavyāmohakārakāḥ 
ekaṃ yadi bhavec chāstraṃ jñānaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ bhavet ।। 

bahutvād iha śātrāṇāṃ jñānatattvaṃ sudurlabham 
āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

idam ekaṃ suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā 
tyaktvā vyāmohakān sarvān tasmāc chāstrārthavistarān ।। 

ananyacetā dhyāyasva nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ 
evaṃ jnātvā tu satataṃ devadevaṃ tam avyayam ।। 

kṣipraṃ yāsyasi tatraiva sāyujyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ 
śrutvedaṃ brahmaṇā proktaṃ jñānayogaṃ sudurlabham ।। 

tato aham āsaṃ viprendra nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti ye vidur brahma śāśvatam ।। 

antakāle japantas te yānti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam 
tasmān nārāyaṇas tāta paramātmā sanātanaḥ ।। 

ananyamanasā nityaṃ dhyeyas tattvavicintakaiḥ 
nārāyaṇo jagadvyāpī paramātmā sanātanaḥ ।। 

jagatāṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhāraparipālanatatparaḥ 
śravaṇāt paṭhanāc caiva nididhyāsanatatparaiḥ ।। 

ārādhyaḥ sarvathā brahman puruṣeṇa hitaiṣiṇā 
niḥspṛhā nityasaṃtuṣṭā jñāninaḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ ।। 

nirmamā nirahaṃkārā rāgadveṣavivarjitāḥ 
apakṣapatitāḥ śāntāḥ sarvasaṃkalpavarjitāḥ ।। 

dhyānayogaparā brahman te paśyanti jagatpatim 
tyaktatrayā mahātmāno vāsudevaṃ hariṃ gurum ।। 

kīrtayanti jagannāthaṃ te paśyanti jagatpatim 
tasmāt tvam api viprendra nārāyaṇaparo bhava ।। 

tadanyaḥ ko mahodāraḥ prārthitaṃ dātum īśvaraḥ 
helayā kīrtito yo vai svaṃ padaṃ diśati dvija ।। 

api kāryas tvayā caiva japaḥ svādhyāya eva ca 
tam evoddiśya deveśaṃ kuru nityam atandritaḥ ।। 

kiṃ tatra bahubhir mantraiḥ kiṃ tatra bahubhir vrataiḥ 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। 

cīravāsā jaṭadhārī tridaṇḍī muṇḍa eva vā 
bhūṣito vā dvijaśreṣṭha na liṅgaṃ dharmakāraṇam ।। 

ye nṛsaṃśā durātmānaḥ pāpācāraratāḥ sadā 
te api yānti paraṃ sthānaṃ narā nārāyaṇāśrayāḥ ।। 

janmāntarasahasreṣu yasya syād buddhir īdṛśī 
dāso aham vāsudevasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।। 

prayāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ 
kiṃ punas tatgataprāṇaḥ puruṣa saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। 

ity uktvā devadevarṣis tatraivāntaradhīyata 
paropakāraniratas trailokyasyaikabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

puṇḍarīko api dharmātmā nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ 
namo astu keśavāyeti punaḥ punar udīrayan ।। 

prasīdasva mahāyoginn idam uccārya sarvadā 
hṛtpuṇḍarīke govindaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya janārdanam ।। 

tapassiddhikare araṇye śālagrāme tapodhanaḥ 
uvāsa ciram ekākī puruṣārthavicakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

svapne api keśavād anyan na paśyati mahātapāḥ 
nidrāpi tasya naivāsīt puruṣārthavirodhinī ।। 

tapasā brahmacaryeṇa śaucena ca viśeṣataḥ 
janmajanmāntarārūḍhasaṃskāreṇa ca sa dvijaḥ ।। 

prasādād devadevasya sarvalokaikasākṣiṇaḥ 
avāpa paramāṃ siddhiṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ vītakalmaṣaḥ ।। 

siṃhavyāghrās tathānye api mṛgāḥ prāṇivihiṃsakāḥ 
virodhaṃ sahajaṃ hitvā sametās tasya saṃnidhau 
nivasanti dvijaśreṣṭha praśāntendriyavṛttayaḥ ।। 

tataḥ kadācid bhagavān puṇḍarīkasya dhīmataḥ 
prādur āsīj jagannāthaḥ puṇḍarīkāyatekṣaṇaḥ ।। 

śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiḥ pītavāsāḥ sragujjvalaḥ 
śrīvatsavakṣāḥ śrīvāsaḥ kaustubhena vibhūṣitaḥ ।। 

āruhya garuḍaṃ śrīmān añjanācalasaṃnibhaḥ 
meruśṛṅgam ivāruḍhaḥ kālameghas taḍiddyutiḥ ।। 

rājatenātapatreṇa muktādāmavilambinā 
virājamāno deveśaś cāmaravyajanādibhiḥ ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaṃ puṇḍarīkaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ 
papāta śirasā bhūmau sādhvasāvanato dvijaḥ ।। 

pipann iva hṛṣīkeśaṃ nayanābhyāṃ samākulaḥ 
jagāma mahatīṃ tṛptiṃ puṇḍarīkas tadānaghaḥ ।। 

tam evālokayan vīraś ciraprārthitadarśanaḥ 
tatas tam āha bhagavān padmanābhas trivikramaḥ ।। 

prīto asmi vatsa bhadraṃ te puṇḍarīka mahāmate 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dāsyāmi yat te manasi vartate ।। 

etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ devadevena bhāṣitam 
idaṃ vijñāpayam āsa puṇḍarīko mahāmatiḥ ।। 

kvāham atyantadurbuddhiḥ kva cātmahitavīkṣaṇam 
yad dhitaṃ mama deveśa tad ājñāpaya mādhava ।। 

evam ukto atha bhagavān suprītaḥ punar abravīt 
puṇḍarīkaṃ mahābhāgaṃ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam ।। 

āgaccha kuśalaṃ te astu mayaiva saha suvrata 
madrūpadhārī nityātmā mamaiva pārṣado bhava ।। 

evam uktavati prītyā śrīdhare bhaktavatsale 
devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।। 

devāḥ sendrās tathā siddhāḥ sādhu sādhv ity athābruvan 
jaguś ca siddhagandharvāḥ kiṃnarāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। 

athainaṃ samupādāya vāsudevo jagatpatiḥ 
jagāma garuḍārūḍhaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ ।। 

tasmāt tvam api viprendra viṣṇubhaktisamanvitaḥ 
taccittas tadgataprāṇas tadbhaktānāṃ hite rataḥ ।। 

arcayitvā yathāyogaṃ bhajasva puruṣottamam 
śṛṇuṣva tatkathāḥ puṇyāḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīḥ ।। 

yenopāyena viprendra viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ 
prīto bhavati viśvātmā tat kuruṣva suvistaram ।। 

aśvamedhasahasreṇa vājapeyaśatair api 
nāpnuvanti gatiṃ puṇyāṃ nārāyaṇaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। 

ajaram amaram ekaṃ dhyeyam ādyantaśūnyaṃ saguṇaviguṇam ādyaṃ sthūlam atyantasūkṣmam 
nirupamam upameyaṃ yogināṃ jñānagamyaṃ tribhuvanagurum īśaṃ tvāṃ prapanno asmi viṣṇo ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe puṇḍarīkanāradasaṃvāde catuḥṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

tvatto hi śrotum icchāmi guhyakṣetrāṇi vai hareḥ 
nāmāni ca suguhyāni vada pāpaharāṇi ca ।। 

mandarasthaṃ hariṃ devaṃ brahmā pṛcchati keśavam 
bhagavantaṃ devadevaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।। 

keṣu keṣu ca kṣetreṣu draṣṭavyo asi mayā hare 
bhaktair anyaiḥ suraśreṣṭha muktikāmair viśeṣataḥ ।। 

yāni te guhyanāmāni kṣetrāṇi ca jagatpate 
tāny ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi tvattaḥ padmāyatekṣaṇa ।। 

kiṃ japan sugatiṃ yāti naro nityam atandritaḥ 
tvadbhaktānāṃ hitārthāya tan me vada sureśvara ।। 

śṛṇuṣvāvahito brahman guhyanāmāni me adhunā 
kṣetrāṇi caiva guhyāni tava vakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।। 

kokāmukhe tu vārāhaṃ mandare madhusūdanam 
anantaṃ kapiladvīpe prabhāse ravinandanam ।। 

mālyodapāne vaikuṇṭhaṃ mahendre tu nṛpātmajam 
ṛṣabhe tu mahāviṣṇuṃ dvārakāyāṃ tu bhūpatim ।। 

pāṇḍusahye tu deveśaṃ vāsurūḍhe jagatpatim 
vallīvaṭe mahāyogaṃ citrakūṭe narādhipam ।। 

nimiṣe pītavāsaṃ ca gavāṃ niṣkramaṇe harim 
śālagrāme tapovāsam acintyaṃ gandhamādane ।। 

kubjāgāre hṛṣīkeśaṃ gandhadvāre payodharam 
garuḍadhvajaṃ tu sakale govindaṃ nāma sāyake ।। 

vṛndāvane tu gopālaṃ mathurāyāṃ svayaṃbhuvam 
kedāre mādhavaṃ vindyād vārāṇasyāṃ tu keśavam ।। 

puṣkare puṣkarākṣaṃ tu dhṛṣṭadyumne jayadhvajam 
tṛṇabinduvane vīram aśokaṃ sindhusāgare ।। 

kaseraṭe mahābāhum amṛtaṃ taijase vane 
viśvāsayūpe viśvaīśaṃ narasiṃhaṃ mahāvane ।। 

halāṅgare ripuharaṃ devaśālāṃ trivikramam 
puruṣottamaṃ daśapure kubjake vāmanaṃ viduḥ ।। 

vidyādharaṃ vitastāyāṃ vārāhe dharaṇīdharam 
devadāruvane guhyaṃ kāveryāṃ nāgaśāyinam ।। 

prayāge yogamūrtiṃ ca payoṣṇyāṃ ca sudarśanam 
kumāratīrthe kaumāraṃ lohite hayaśīrṣakam ।। 

ujjayinyāṃ trivikramaṃ liṅgakūṭe caturbhujam 
hariharaṃ tu bhadrāyāṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate ।। 

viśvarūpaṃ kurukṣetre maṇikuṇḍe halāyudham 
lokanātham ayodhyāyāṃ kuṇḍine kuṇḍineśvaram ।। 

bhāṇḍāre vāsudevaṃ tu cakratīrthe sudarśanam 
āḍhye viṣṇupadaṃ vidyāc chūkare śūkaraṃ viduḥ ।। 

brahmeśaṃ mānase tīrthe daṇḍake śyāmalaṃ viduḥ 
trikūṭe nāgamokṣaṃ ca merupṛṣṭhe ca bhāskaram ।। 

virajaṃ puṣpabhadrāyāṃ bālaṃ keralake viduḥ 
yaśaskaraṃ vipāśāyāṃ māhiṣmatyāṃ hutāśanam ।। 

kṣīrābdhau padmanābhaṃ tu vimale tu sanātanam 
śivanadyāṃ śivakaraṃ gayāyāṃ ca gadādharam ।। 

sarvatra paramātmānaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa mucyate 
aṣṭaṣaṣṭiś ca nāmāni kathitāni mayā tava ।। 

kṣetrāṇi caiva guhyāni kathitāni viśeṣataḥ 
etāni mama nāmāni rahasyāni prajāpate ।। 

yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya śṛṇuyād vāpi nityaśaḥ 
gavāṃ śatasahasrasya dattasya phalam āpnuyāt ।। 

dine dine śucir bhūtvā nāmāny etāni yaḥ paṭhet 
duḥsvapnaṃ na bhavet tasya matprasādān na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

aṣṭaṣaṣṭis tu nāmāni trikālaṃ yaḥ paṭhen naraḥ 
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo mama loke sa modate ।। 

draṣṭavyāni yathāśaktyā kṣetrāṇy etāni mānavaiḥ 
vaiṣṇavais tu viśeṣeṇa teṣām muktiṃ dadāmy aham ।। 

hariṃ samabhyarcya tadagrasaṃsthito hariṃ smaran viṣṇudine viśeṣataḥ 
imaṃ stavaṃ yaḥ paṭhate sa mānavaḥ prāpnoti viṣṇor amṛtātmakaṃ padam ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ādye dharmārthamokṣadāyini viṣṇuvallabhe pañcaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

uktaḥ puṇyaḥ stavo brahman harer ebhis ca nāmabhiḥ 
punar anyāni nāmāni yāni tāni nibodha me ।। 

gaṅgā tu prathamaṃ puṇyā yamunā gomatī punaḥ 
sarayūḥ sarasvatī ca candrabhāgā carmaṇvatī ।। 

kurukṣetraṃ gayā caiva puṣkarāṇi tathārbudam 
narmadā ca mahāpuṇyā tīrthāny etāni cottare ।। 

tāpī payoṣṇī puṇye dve tatsaṅgāt tīrtham uttamam 
tathā brahmagireś cāpi mekhalābhiḥ samanvitāḥ ।। 

virajaṃ ca tathā tīrthaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram 
godāvarī mahāpuṇyā sarvatra caturānana ।। 

tuṅgabhadrā mahāpuṇyā yatrāhaṃ kamalodbhava 
hareṇa sārdhaṃ prītyā tu vasāmi munipūjitaḥ ।। 

dakṣiṇagaṅgā kṛṣṇā tu kāverī ca viśeṣataḥ 
sahye tv āmalakagrāme sthito ahaṃ kamalodbhava ।। 

devadevasya nāmnā tu tvayā brahman sadārcitaḥ 
tatra tīrthāny anekāni sarvapāpaharāṇi vai 
yeṣu snātvā ca pītvā ca pāpān mucyati mānavaḥ ।। 

ity evaṃ kathayitvā tu tīrthāni madhusūdanaḥ 
brahmaṇe gatavān brahman brahmāpi svapuraṃ gataḥ ।। 

tasminn āmalakagrāme puṇyatīrthāni yāni vai 
tāni me vada dharmajña vistareṇa yathārthataḥ ।। 

kṣetrotpattiṃ ca māhātmyaṃ yātrāparvaṃ ca yatra tat 
tatrāsau devadeveśaḥ pūjyate brahmaṇā svayam ।। 

śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi puṇyaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam 
sahyāmalakatīrthasya utpattyādi mahāmune ।। 

purā sahyavanoddeśe tarur āmalako mahān 
āsīd brahman mahogro ayaṃ nāmnāyaṃ cocyate budhaiḥ ।। 

phalāni tasya vṛkṣasya mahānti surasāni ca 
darśanīyāni divyāni durlabhāni mahāmune ।। 

pareṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ tu pareṇa brahmaṇā purā 
sa dṛṣṭas tu mahāvṛkṣo mahāphalasamanvitaḥ ।। 

kim etad iti viprendra dhyānadṛṣṭiparo abhavat 
dhyānena dṛṣṭavāṃs tatra punar āmalakaṃ tarum ।। 

tasyopari tu deveśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam 
utthāya ca punaḥ paśyet pratimām eva kevalām ।। 

tatpādaṃ bhūtale devaḥ praviveśa mahātaruḥ 
tatas tv ārādhayāmasa devadeveśam avyayam ।। 

gandhapuṣpādibhir nityaṃ brahmā lokapitamahaḥ 
dvādaśabhiḥ saptabhis tu saṃkhyābhiḥ pujito hariḥ ।। 

tasmin kṣetre muniśreṣṭha māhātmyaṃ tasya ko vadet 
śrīsahyāmalakagrāme devadeveśam avyayam ।। 

ārādhya tīrthe saṃprāptā dvādaśa prati caturmukham 
tasya pādatale tīrthaṃ niḥsṛtaṃ paścimāmukham ।। 

tac cakratīrtham abhavat puṇyaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam 
cakratirthe naraḥ snātvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 

bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi brahmaloke mahīyate 
śaṅkhatīrthe naraḥ snātvā vājapeyaphalaṃ labhet ।। 

pauṣe māse tu puṣyārke tadyātrādivasaṃ mune 
brahmaṇaḥ kuṇḍikā pūrvaṃ gaṅgātoyaprapūritā ।। 

tasyādrau patitā brahmaṃs tatra tīrthe aśubhaṃ haret 
nāmnā tatkuṇḍikātīrthaṃ śilāgṛhasamanvitam ।। 

tattīrthe manujaḥ snātvā tadānīṃ siddhim āpnuyāt 
trirātropoṣito bhūtvā yas tatra snāti mānavaḥ ।। 

sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate 
kuṇḍikātīrthād uttare piṇḍasthānāc ca dakṣiṇe ।। 

ṛṇamocanatīrthaṃ hi tīrthānāṃ guhyam uttamam 
trirātram uṣito yas tu tatra snānaṃ samācaret ।। 

ṛṇais tribhir asau brahman mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā pitṛbhyaś ca piṇḍasthāneṣu yo narah ।। 

pitṝn uddiśya vidhivat piṇḍān nirvāpayiṣyati 
sutṛptāḥ pitaro yānti pitṛlokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

pañcarātroṣitasnāyī tīrthe vai pāpamocane 
sarvapāpakṣayaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke sa modate ।। 

tatraiva mahatīṃ dhārāṃ śirasā yas tu dhārayet 
sarvakratuphalaṃ prāpya nākapṛṣṭhe mahīyate ।। 

dhanuḥpāte mahātīrthe bhaktyā yaḥ snānam ācaret 
āyurbhogaphalaṃ prāpya svargaloke mahīyate ।। 

śarabindau naraḥ snātvā śatakratupuraṃ vrajet 
vārāhatīrthe viprendra sahye yaḥ snānam ācaret ।। 

ahorātroṣito bhūtvā viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
ākāśagaṅgānāmnā ca sahyāgre tīrtham uttamam ।। 

śilātalāt tato brahman nirgatā śvetamṛttikā 
tasyāṃ bhaktyā tu yaḥ snāti naro dvijavarottamam ।। 

sarvakratuphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
brahmann amalasahyādrer yadyadtoyavinirgamaḥ ।। 

tatra tīrthaṃ vijānīhi snātvā pāpāt pramucyate 
sahyādriṃ gatavān nityaṃ snātvā pāpāt pramucyate ।। 

eteṣu tīrtheṣu naro dvijendra puṇyeṣu sahyādrisamudbhaveṣu 
dattvā supuṣpāṇi hariṃ sa bhaktyā vihāya pāpaṃ praviśet sa viṣṇum ।। 

sakṛt tīrthādritoyeṣu gaṅgāyāṃ tu punah punaḥ 
sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvadevamayo hariḥ ।। 

sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadharmo dayāparaḥ 
evaṃ te kathitaṃ vipra kṣetramāhātmyam uttamam ।। 

śrīsahyāmalakagrāme tīrthe snātvā phalāni ca 
tīrthānām api yat tīrthaṃ tat tīrthaṃ dvijasattama 
devadevasya pādasya talād bhuvi niniḥsṛtam ।। 

ambhoyugaṃ turagamedhasahasratulyaṃ tac cakratīrtham iti vedavido vadanti 
snānāc ca tatra manujā na punar bhavanti pādau praṇamya śirasā madhusūdanasya ।। 

gaṅgāprayāgagamanaimiṣapuṣkarāṇi puṇyāyutāni kurujāṅgalayāmunāni 
kālena tīrthasalilāni punanti pāpāt pādodakaṃ bhagavatas tu punāti sadyaḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapuraṇe tīrthapraśaṃsāyāṃ ṣaṭsaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

tīrthāni kathitāny evaṃ bhaumāni dvijasattama 
mānasāni hi tīrthāni phaladāni viśeṣataḥ ।। 

manonirmalatā tīrthaṃ rāgādibhir anākulā 
satyaṃ tīrthaṃ dayā tīrthaṃ tīrtham indriyanigrahaḥ ।। 

guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ mātṛśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathā 
svadharmācaraṇaṃ tīrthaṃ tīrtham agner upāsanam ।। 

etāni puṇyatīrthāni vratāni śṛṇu me adhunā 
ekabhuktaṃ tathā naktam upavāsaṃ ca vai mune ।। 

pūrṇamāsyām amāvāsyām ekabhuktaṃ samācaret 
tatraikabhuktaṃ kurvāṇaḥ puṇyāṃ gatim avāpnuyāt ।। 

caturthyāṃ tu caturdaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ naktam ācaret 
aṣṭamyāṃ tu trayodaśyāṃ sa prāpnoty abhivāñchitam ।। 

upavāso manuśreṣṭha ekādaśyāṃ vidhīyate 
narasiṃhaṃ samabhyarcya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 

hastayukte arkadivase sauranaktaṃ samācaret 
snātvārkamadhye viṣṇuṃ ca dhyātvā rogāt pramucyate ।। 

ātmano dviguṇāṃ chāyāṃ yadā saṃtiṣṭhate raviḥ 
sauranaktaṃ vijānīyān na naktaṃ niśi bhojanam ।। 

guruvāre trayodaśyām aparāhṇe jale tataḥ 
tarpayitvā pitṛn devān ṛṣīṃś ca tilatandulaiḥ ।। 

narasiṃhaṃ samabhyarcya yaḥ karoty upavāsakam 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। 

yadāgastyodaye prāpte tadā saptasu rātriṣu 
arghyaṃ dadyāt samabhyarcya agastyāya mahāmune ।। 

śaṅkhe toyaṃ vinikṣipya sitapuṣpākṣatair yutam 
mantreṇānena vai dadyāc chitapuṣpādinārcite ।। 

kāśapuṣpapratīkāśa agnimārutasaṃbhava 
mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putra kumbhayone namo astu te ।। 

ātāpī bhakṣito yena vātāpī ca mahāsuraḥ 
samudraḥ śoṣito yena so agastyaḥ prīyatāṃ mama ।। 

evaṃ tu dadyād yo sarvam agastye vai diśaṃ prati 
sarvapāpavinirmuktas tamas tarati dustaram ।। 

evaṃ te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bharadvāja mahāmune 
purāṇaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ ca munīnāṃ saṃnidhau mayā ।। 

sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṃso manvantarāṇi ca 
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva sarvam eva prakīrtitam ।। 

brahmaṇaiva purā proktaṃ marīcyādiṣu vai mune 
tebhyaś ca bhṛguṇā proktaṃ mārkaṇḍeyāya vai tataḥ ।। 

mārkaṇḍeyena vai proktaṃ rājño nāgakulasya ha 
prasādān narasiṃhasya prāptaṃ vyāsena dhīmatā ।। 

tatprasādān mayā prāptaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
purāṇaṃ narasiṃhasya mayā ca kathitaṃ tava ।। 

munīnāṃ saṃnidhau puṇyaṃ svasti te astu vrajāmy aham 
yaḥ śṛṇoti śucir bhūtvā purāṇaṃ hy etad uttamam ।। 

māghe māsi prayāge tu sa snānaphalam āpnuyāt 
yo bhaktyā śrāvayed bhaktān nityaṃ naraharer idam ।। 

sarvatīrthaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
śrutvaivaṃ snātakaiḥ sārdhaṃ bharadvājo mahāmatiḥ ।। 

sūtam abhyarcya tatraiva sthitavān munayo gatāḥ 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ nṛsiṃhātmakam ।। 

paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ nṛṇāṃ narasiṃho prasīdati 
prasanne devadeveśe sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet ।। 

prakṣīṇapāpabandhās te muktiṃ yānti narā iti ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe mānasatīrthavrataṃ nāma saptaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।

ity etat sarvam ākhyātaṃ purāṇaṃ nārasiṃhakam 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaduḥkhanivāraṇam ।। 

samastapuṇyaphaladaṃ sarvayajñaphalapradam 
ye paṭhanty api śṛṇvanti ślokaṃ ślokārdham eva vā ।। 

na teṣāṃ pāpabandhas tu kadācid api jāyate 
viṣṇvarpitam idaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ sarvakāmadam ।। 

bhaktyā ca vadatām etac chṛṇvatāṃ ca phalaṃ śṛṇu 
śatajanmārjitaiḥ pāpaiḥ sadya eva vimocitāḥ ।। 

sahasrakulasaṃyuktāḥ prayānti paramaṃ padam 
kiṃ tīrthair gopradānair vā tapobhir vā kim adhvaraiḥ ।। 

ahanyahani govindaṃ tatparatvena śṛṇvatām 
yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya yad asya ślokaviṃśatim ।। 

jyotiṣṭomaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
etat pavitraṃ pūjyaṃ ca na vācyam akṛtātmanām ।। 

dvijānāṃ viṣṇubhaktānāṃ śrāvyam etan na saṃśayaḥ 
etat purāṇaśravaṇam ihāmutra sukhapradam ।। 

vadatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ sadyaḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
bahunātra kim uktena bhūyo bhūyo munīśvarāḥ ।। 

śraddhayāśraddhayā vāpi śrotavyam idam uttamam 
bhāradvājamukhāḥ sarve kṛtakṛtyā dvijottamāḥ ।। 

sūtaṃ hṛṣṭāḥ prapūjyātha sarve svasvāśramaṃ yayuḥ ।। 

।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sūtabharadvājādisaṃvāde sarvaduḥkhopaharaṃ śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇasya māhātmyaṃ samāptam ।। narp ।।
